## January 6, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
* In the morning, the fourth meeting of the 13th CPPCC Wuhan Committee opened. Ma Guoqiang, secretary of the Wuhan Municipal Party Committee, attended the conference and delivered a speech. Ma Xuming, vice chairman of the Hubei Provincial Committee of the Chinese People's Political Consultative Conference, delivered a speech on behalf of the Provincial Committee of the Chinese People's Political Consultative Conference. Mayor Zhou Xianwang and Minister of the Organization Department Hu Lishan attended the conference and took a seat on the rostrum. See [Yangtze River Network](http://news.cjn.cn/sywh/202001/t3528217.htm). <br>
* A severely ill patient from Huanggang who had difficulty breathing was rejected by many hospitals and sent to the emergency department of Wuhan University Zhongnan Hospital. Peng Zhiyong, director of the Department of Critical Care Medicine, participated in the consultation and informed the dean that the patient is likely to infect others. It must be strict Take isolation measures in accordance with the infectious disease protection method, evacuate other patients in the ward, rebuild the ward according to SARS standards, and isolate the living area of ​​medical staff from the patients. It is for the hospital to receive the first unidentified pneumonia patient. See February 5th [Caixin.com:Critical Physicians: How we rescue critical patients](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/IlQyOfQtsyvpptPAlTjwPg), "Sanlian Life Weekly", 2020 Phase 7 [New Coronary Pneumonia, the node of the hospital](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/138). <br>
* A respiratory physician at the Hubei Provincial Hospital of Integrated Traditional Chinese and Western Medicine (ie, Xinhua Hospital in Hubei Province) had an abnormal phenomenon. The lung CT showed a small shadow, which was ground glass. The doctor did not contact the South China Seafood Market. On the same day, the Xinhua Hospital convened the heads of various departments to have a meeting. The director of the department communicates the instructions of the hospital and must not disclose the relevant information to the outside world, especially the media. See February 3rd [Caixin.com:Cover report, one of the scenes: Wuhan Besieged_Caixin Weekly Channel] interviewed Li Huahua, a radiologist at Xinhua Hospital. <br>
* The Hubei Provincial Health Commission has transferred medical staff from Wuhan to support Wuhan Jinyintan Hospital. February 9 [Yangtze River Daily:Huang Chaolin: Use 6 identities and viruses in 42 days](http://cjrb.cjn.cn/html/2020-02/09/content_164342.htm). <br>
* Hubei Provincial Health and Welfare Committee official WeChat public account [Health Hubei](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/7XNck2ZZSygZ5XR4hh5rsQ) reproduced an interview with Yang Gang Daily reporter Li Gang, a disease control expert and director of Wuhan Center for Disease Control and Prevention . Li Gang said that "pathogen identification and etiology tracing work are still in progress, and no clear evidence of human-to-human transmission has been found." <br>
* On the same day, Jiang Chaoliang, secretary of the Hubei Provincial Party Committee, visited a community health service center in Jianghan District. He was wearing a mask. Dean Fang Han recalled that in those days, we asked our medical staff to wear masks. Accompanying them were the secretary of the Wuhan Municipal Party Committee, the secretary of the District Party Committee and the people of the Wuhan Municipal Health and Health Committee. At that time, the leadership conveyed the meaning of "preventable and controllable", "to prevent and control medical personnel, and to prevent infection of medical personnel." But since then, the work of the community health service center has not changed, until the 29th of the year (January 23) is a normal consultation. See March 7 [Eight o'clock news:Wuhan's first line of defense-how did the community health service center fail? ](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/150#issue-577432320). <br>

## January 7, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
* In the morning, [the fifth meeting of the 14th Wuhan People's Congress](http://www.whrd.gov.cn/html/rdyw/2020/0108/16938.shtml) opened. Municipal Party Committee Secretary Ma Guoqiang presided over the meeting, and Mayor Zhou Xianwang made a government work report to the meeting. <br>
* At 21:00, the [National Expert Panel on Preliminary Evaluation of Pathogen Test Results](http://www.xinhuanet.com/2020-01/09/c_1125438971.htm) laboratory obtained the whole genome sequence of the new coronavirus, " The pathogen of the "unexplained viral pneumonia" case was initially determined to be a new coronavirus. A total of 15 cases of positive results of novel coronavirus were detected by nucleic acid detection method, and the virus was isolated from a sample of positive patients. "A novel coronavirus outbreak of global health concern" ["new coronavirus outbreak of global health concern"](https://www.thelancet.com/journals/lancet/article/PIIS0140-6736 ( 20) 30185-9 / fulltext) also mentioned this date. <br>
* Lu Jun, an emergency physician at Wuhan Tongji Hospital, had a patchy and ground glass-like lesion on his lungs during the reexamination, and was later diagnosed as "unexplained viral pneumonia." See February 3rd [Caixin.com:One of the cover reports on the scene: Wuhan Fortress](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/56#issue-558835473) Liu Li interviewed the recollection. <br>
* Patient Wang Mou, who had no obvious improvement in intubation and rescue in the Union Hospital, was transferred to Jinyintan Hospital 3 days later, and was diagnosed as "severe pneumonia with acute respiratory distress syndrome" by five experts with different opinions because of no etiological evidence , Septic shock and other complications, accompanied by primary hypertension "died. The doctor told his family that he was the first patient to die in this outbreak. His sister, daughter, and son-in-law also had symptoms similar to him. See March 5th [Southern Weekend ｜ "Restructuring" Jinyintan: The Secret of the Epidemic Storm Eye](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/146). <br>
* On the same day, a patient who went to the hospital for flu-like illness was determined to be a new coronary pneumonia by nucleic acid detection of researchers at Wuhan Disease Control Center. She developed the disease on the 4th, see [Wen-Hua Kong, Yao Li, Ming- Wei Peng, et al. SARS-CoV-2 detection in patients with influenza-like illness. * Nature Microbiology *, Apr 7, 2020 (SARS-CoV-2 detection in patients with influenza-like illness)](https: // www .nature.com / articles / s41564-020-0713-1). The article also pointed out that there were 3 and 5 new crown patients among the patients who went to the clinic on January 13 and 21, respectively. <br>

## January 8, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
* In the morning, [The Third Meeting of the 13th CPPCC Wuhan Committee](http://news.cjn.cn/tfsj/2019whlh/ttxw_16360/201901/t3336166.htm) closed. <br>
* In the afternoon, the [Fourth Session of the Fourteenth People ’s Congress of Wuhan](http://news.cjn.cn/tfsj/2019whlh/ttxw_16360/201901/t3336229.htm) closed after successfully completing the various agendas. <br>
* Li Wenliang, Department of Ophthalmology, Wuhan Central Hospital, was infected after receiving an 82-year-old female glaucoma patient. According to Affin, the emergency department, when he was admitted, "he did not have special protection, and the patient did not get fever when he came, so he was careless." See February 17 [China News Weekly:Personal experience: Medical staff of Wuhan Central Hospital The beginning and end of infection](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/106#issue-566625534). <br>
* Central South Hospital received the first patient with unknown pneumonia and transferred to the intensive care unit. Because many hospitals received written or oral instructions from higher authorities to warn of "attention to impact", the medical care during transportation did not provide other protection except that everyone wore a mask. According to Hu Bo, deputy director of the Department of Critical Care Medicine, "someone got infected later." See "Sanlian Life Weekly" 2020 No. 7 [New Coronary Pneumonia, Hospital Node](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/138). <br>

【China】 <br>
* In the evening, the second group of experts from the National Health Commission began to arrive in Wuhan one after another (Wang Guangfa arrived in the evening on the 8th, and Zeng Guang in the morning on the 9th), and returned to January 16. Currently known members of this group of experts are Wang Guangfa, director of the Department of Respiratory and Critical Care Medicine, Peking University First Hospital (in the medical treatment group), Jiang Rongmeng, chief physician of the Second Department of Infection, Ditan Hospital, Gao Zhancheng, director of the Department of Respiratory Medicine, Peking University People's Hospital Feng Zijian, deputy director of the Control Center, Yang Weizhong, former deputy director, and Zeng Guang, chief scientist of epidemiology at the Chinese Center for Disease Control and Prevention. See February 2 [Freezing Point Weekly:Wang Guang, a member of the Expert Committee of the Health and Health Commission, was issued to the hospital and answered our 8 questions](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/DWcRVz10zps27VIrml_Khg), February 5 [ China News Weekly:Regrets of Wuhan: How did the golden prevention and control period miss? ](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/90#issue-562954124) and February 11 [Universal People:Zeng Guang: The battle in Wuhan started on the premise of unclear boundaries between the enemy and us ](http://www.hqrw.com.cn/2020/0211/92941.shtml). <br>
* In the afternoon, a 60-year-old female fever patient was admitted to the Guangdong Academy of Traditional Chinese Medicine Xueyuan Social Welfare Center. The patient reported that she had not left Shenzhen recently, but six of her relatives were from December 29 to 2019. On January 4, 2020, he visited Wuhan to visit relatives, which caused the alert of Shenzhen Disease Control System. Four of the six relatives had already had onset before. They were admitted to the Shenzhen Hospital of the University of Hong Kong on January 10-11, and tested positive for new coronavirus nucleic acids around the 14th. The patient was also admitted to Shenzhen Hospital on January 14 and tested positive for the novel coronavirus nucleic acid on the 15th. The patient ’s lack of travel history in Wuhan prompted the ability of the new coronavirus to spread from person to person, aroused the alert of Academician Yuan Guoyong of Shenzhen Hospital, and reported the situation to Guangdong Province and China CDC in writing on January 17. See entry on January 17]. See [Jasper Fuk-Woo Chan, et. A familial cluster of pneumonia associated with the 2019 novel coronavirus indicating person-to-person transmission: a study of a family cluster. The Lancet, Jan. 24, 2020 (and the 2019 new crown A virus-associated case of family cluster pneumonia indicates the spread of the virus from person to person: a study of family cluster cases)](https://www.thelancet.com/journals/lancet/article/PIIS0140-6736(20)30154- 9 / fulltext), January 27 [Financial Magazine:Expert Committee of National Health and Health Commission Yuan Guoyong: "Wuhan pneumonia" still needs to determine a more accurate fatality rate](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/mrulHdV7HwSi2ImuEzYfng ) And February 25 [Southern Metropolis Daily:Details disclosed! Guangdong's first "onset" family confirmed the diagnosis process](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/ry0Mo5coz_zszsOJJuKylA). <br>

## January 9, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
* Wuhan Virus Research Institute indicates that the virus resource has been included in the national virus resource library according to the standard and has been standardized for deposit (deposit number: IVCAS 6.7512), which can be provided to relevant institutions in accordance with laws and regulations, and will be the current 2019 new coronavirus Scientific research, vaccine development, biomedical screening, etc. provide important resource support. See Wuhan Institute of Virology, Chinese Academy of Sciences [Wuhan Institute of Virology is fully committed to research on new coronavirus pneumonia](http://www.whiov.ac.cn/xwdt_105286/zhxw/202001/t20200129_5494574.html). <br>
* Zeng Guang worked in Wuhan and had "basic no intersection" with other experts of the National Health and Health Commission in Wuhan at that time, mainly listening to some briefings from Hubei Province and Wuhan City. He recalled, "They said that the (patient) condition is relatively mild, which is similar to seasonal pneumonia, and none of the hundreds of close contacts have the disease. It is very easy to say." He remembered when he heard of the "limited person-to-person" phenomenon , But only individual people. 【China】 <br>

Xu Jianguo said, "A new coronavirus was detected in the laboratory, and the whole genome sequence of the virus was obtained. A total of 15 cases of positive results of the new coronavirus were detected by nucleic acid detection methods. The virus was isolated from a sample of positive patients. Electron microscopy The typical coronavirus morphology is shown below, "The pathogen of this unexplained viral pneumonia is initially determined as a new coronavirus", "The next step is to conduct expert research and judgment based on pathogenic research, epidemiological investigation and clinical manifestations." , [CCTV News](https://weibo.com/2656274875/IoE0ZyrWd) has public reports. <br>

## January 10, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
* The Central South Hospital of Wuhan University reported the serious situation that the 16 beds prepared by the ICU of the unknown pneumonia infectious disease were full to the Wuhan Municipal Health and Health Commission. See February 5th [Caixin.com:Critical Physician: How we rescue critical patients](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/IlQyOfQtsyvpptPAlTjwPg). <br>
* Wuhan Youfu Hospital reported a large number of medical staff and patients who did not meet the diagnostic criteria of "unexplained viral pneumonia" to the higher-level disease control department. According to a doctor's recall, the superior disease control department did not come to the hospital for investigation immediately, but instead asked them: "You have not been in contact with the South China seafood market, why is there this disease?" Youfu Hospital gave feedback to the three cases of the initial physician consultation To the superior disease control department, the latter is neither affirmed nor denied. See February 11 [Eight o'clock Jianwen:Lost Opportunity, Case of Small Hospital Early Neglected in New Crown Outbreak](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/91). <br>
* The first case of medical staff was found in the emergency department of Wuhan City Central Hospital. It was a nurse in Houhu District. Emergency department Ivan recalled, "We later analyzed that she may not wear a mask well." See February 17 [China News Weekly:Personal experience tells: the beginning and end of infection of medical staff in Wuhan Central Hospital](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/106#issue-566625534). <br>
* Around January 10, Wuhan Central Hospital reported a group of patients with unexplained pneumonia to Jianghan District CDC. Wang Wenyong found that one patient had no consultation form and asked the hospital for the reason and was informed that there was no consultation information. Wang Wenyong called the hospital and said that this did not comply with the reporting process, and proposed to modify the patient's condition from unexplained pneumonia to other cases. Wang Wenyong recalled afterwards, "At that time, the city already told us that you still have to guide the hospital to make a diagnosis and report of unexplained pneumonia, and you need to" report with caution. "Now, it may be wrong at the time, but it is true. This is the above policy, and we cannot say too much. Because our disease control actually does not have the so-called power, it is to act according to the requirements. When there are any requirements on the above, we can still only do according to the requirements, not to say Follow your own. "See April 2 [China News Weekly · Back to Wuhan Primary Disease Control Director: No one expected this disease to be so ruthless](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/ 172 # issue-593162687). <br>
* The Ministry of Science and Technology urgently launched four major research projects on new coronary pneumonia. Among them, the clinical project undertaken by Jinyintan Hospital started today, and Huang Chaolin is one of the persons in charge. According to later memories, the patient may be exposed to infection when seeing the relatives of the patient that day. See February 9 [Yangtze River Daily:Huang Chaolin: Contest with 6 identities and viruses in 42 days](http://cjrb.cjn.cn/html/2020-02/09/content_164342.htm).

【China】 <br>
* Spring Festival begins. <br>
* [Wenjian Medical](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/6#issue-556820423) decided to mobilize 380 people in the subsidiary ’s only mask workshop, and to produce N95 masks and surgical masks without holiday during the Spring Festival And nursing masks. <br>
* Shenzhen Futian District CDC held a personal protection training course for emergency response personnel of severe respiratory infectious diseases. At that time, information on the source, transmission route, and susceptible population of New Coronary Pneumonia had not yet been determined. That night, the Shenzhen University Hospital of Hong Kong received two fever patients. This is the first case reported in Shenzhen, and the first case is a family-aggregated infection. Shenzhen sounded the alarm. See March 1st [Caixin.com:Special Feature:How to draw the conclusion of “People-to-Man” in Shenzhen](http://china.caixin.com/2020-03-01/101522553.html). <br>
* In the evening, Wang Guangfa said in an interview with Xinhua News Agency that the current patient's condition and the overall epidemic situation are under control, and most of the patients' condition is mild to moderate. The following day [Xinhua Weibo](https://weibo.com/2810373291/IoXuKxSPG) reprinted the report. <br>

【International】 <br>
* The World Health Organization issued [International Travel and Sanitation Recommendations](https://www.who.int/ith/2020-0901_outbreak_of_Pneumonia_caused_by_a_new_coronavirus_in_C/en/), saying that it has not received reports of infections outside Wuhan and passengers are not recommended to take any Specific health measures suggest that no travel or trade restrictions should be imposed on China. The synchronized [tweet](https://twitter.com/WHO/status/1215320529059688449) map is still coronavirus. <br>
* The World Health Organization issued [Surveillance case definitions for human infection with novel coronavirus](https://apps.who.int/iris/bitstream/handle/10665/330376/WHO-2019 -nCoV-Surveillance-v2020.1-eng.pdf? sequence = 5 & isAllowed = y), and [Laboratory testing of human suspected cases of novel coronavirus (nCoV) infection](https: / /apps.who.int/iris/bitstream/handle/10665/330374/WHO-2019-nCoV-laboratory-2020.1-eng.pdf). The first document clarified that the main monitoring purpose was to monitor and identify cases of infection with new coronaviruses, and to look for evidence of expanded or sustained human-to-human transmission. The report indicates that the clinical characterization of the disease, the severity spectrum, and the course of the disease need to be further determined; the epidemiological characteristics of the virus, such as how to spread it, and the risk factor, need to be followed up. The second document points out that the pathogen of Wuhan pneumonia has not been finally confirmed, but a new β-coronavirus has been bred from at least one pneumonia patient and characterized by electron microscopy and gene sequence. The same virus was detected in another 15 patients by polymerase chain reaction. The complete genome sequence and other information about the putative pathogen and the detection method for the virus will be given soon. <br>
* [British Guardian](https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/jan/09/chinas-sars-like-illness-worries-health-experts): According to Chinese official announcement, new pneumonia There is no high contagion like SARS among people, nor a 35% fatality rate like the Middle East fever (Mers). No one is currently dead. <br>

## January 11, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
* In the early morning, the Wuhan Municipal Health Commission issued the [Fourth Announcement](http://www.nhc.gov.cn/yjb/s3578/202001/1beb46f061704372b7ca41ef3e682229.shtml), stating that "the existing patient specimens were tested, As of 24:00 on January 10, 2020, pathogenic nucleic acid testing has been completed "(National Centers for Disease Control and Prevention provided PCR reagents to Wuhan)," 41 cases of pneumonia with a preliminary diagnosis of new coronavirus infection, including 2 cases discharged from hospital and severe cases 7 One case, one death, and the remaining patients are in stable condition, "stating that" no new cases have been found since January 3, 2020. At present, no infections by medical personnel have been found, and no clear evidence of human-to-human transmission has been found. " [CCTV News](https://weibo.com/2656274875/IoWrwpsE1) full text reprint announcement. [China CDC](http://www.chinacdc.cn/jkzt/crb/zl/szkb_11803/jszl_11809/202001/t20200119_211274.html) full text reprint announcement.
The patient who died in this announcement was "The Lancet" [A novel coronavirus outbreak of global health concern](https://www.thelancet.com/journals/lancet/article/ PIIS0140-6736 (20) 30185-9 / fulltext) contains the "first example". <br>
According to Wang Guang's post-mortem recall, "41 confirmed cases, including two clustered cases. We have consulted with CDC experts. Based on the two clustered cases, we cannot reach the conclusion of 'person-to-person'. Learn experts to answer. " See February 2 [Bingdian Weekly:Wang Guang, a member of the Expert Committee of the Health and Welfare Committee, was issued to the hospital and answered our 8 questions](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/DWcRVz10zps27VIrml_Khg) <br>
* At the same time, the Wuhan Municipal Health and Health Commission issued [Experts Interpreting the Latest Notification of Unexplained Viral Pneumonia](http://wjw.wuhan.gov.cn/front/web/showDetail/2020011109036), stating that "all close contacts so far None of them, including medical staff, found related cases. " <br>
* In the morning, [The Third Meeting of the 12th Hubei Provincial Committee of the Chinese People ’s Political Consultative Conference](http://www.hubei.gov.cn/zwgk/hbyw/hbywqb/202001/t20200112_1910812.shtml) in Wuhan Hongshan Auditorium Grand opening. Jiang Chaoliang, Secretary of the Hubei Provincial Party Committee of the Communist Party of China, Wang Xiaodong, Governor of the CPC, and Ma Guoqiang, Secretary of the Wuhan Municipal Committee, congratulated the meeting. <br>

【China】 <br>
* In the morning, Professor Zhang Yongzhen of the Shanghai Public Health Clinical Center team member Professor Edward Holmes of the University of Sydney represented the research team at [virological.org website](http://virological.org/t/novel-2019- coronavirus-genome / 319) has released the whole genome sequence of the new coronavirus, which is the earliest scientific researcher to share relevant data with the world [see the entries on December 20 and January 5]. According to January 24 [Wenhui Daily report](https://wenhui.whb.cn/zhuzhanapp/kjwz/20200124/317317.html), the P3 laboratory of Shanghai Public Health Clinical Center was approved by the state on January 24. Increase the qualification of new coronaviruses to study where the virus originates, how the virus spreads, and drug sensitivity. However, according to some other media reports, after January 12, for unknown reasons, the P3 laboratory of the Shanghai Public Health Clinical Center reapplied for the cultivation of live viruses and other related studies cannot be approved, only some clinical tests can be done . It was even ordered to be closed and rectified by the Shanghai Municipal Health and Health Commission. The staff of the center submitted at least four applications to reopen the laboratory. No response has been received so far. See February 25 [Finance Magazine:Research shows that the new coronavirus may appear in November last year, with little recent variation](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/0QwyA3m4U-kahPQW4UMoSw), February 26 [ Caixin.com:New Coronavirus Gene Sequencing Traceability: When the alarm sounded](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/132), February 28 [South China Morning Post:First with the world The Chinese laboratory sharing the coronavirus gene sequence was ordered to close the "rectification", which hindered the research of its new coronavirus pneumonia](https://www.scmp.com/news/china/society/article/3052966/chinese-laboratory -first-shared-coronavirus-genome-world-ordered). <br>
* In the evening, the National Health and Health Commission announced that it will share the gene sequence information of the new coronavirus detected in unexplained viral pneumonia cases in Wuhan with the World Health Organization, and appoint relevant institutions (China Center for Disease Control, Chinese Academy of Medical Sciences and Wuhan virus of Chinese Academy of Sciences) In the Global Influenza Data Database (GISAID, Global Initiative on Sharing All Influenza Data), the viral genome sequences of different patients are shared. The World Health Organization announced on January 12th local time to confirm receipt of the data shared by China, and temporarily named the virus name 2019-nCov. See the National Health and Health Commission [Announcement](http://www.nhc.gov.cn/gjhzs/s7952/202001/422796acaea746549f93e617ccc348a1.shtml), Wuhan Institute of Virology, Chinese Academy of Sciences [Wuhan Institute of Virology](http://www.whiov.ac.cn/xwdt_105286/zhxw/202001/t20200129_5494574.html), February 26 [Caixin Network:New Coronavirus Gene Sequencing Traceability: When Is the Alarm Raised](https : //github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/132) and the World Health Organization [twitter bulletin](https://twitter.com/WHO/status/1216108498188230657). <br>

【International】 <br>
* The World Health Organization [twitter](https://twitter.com/WHO/status/1215981049869668353) provides guidance for medical staff to follow up patients, laboratory tests, disease control, and information disclosure. <br>
* [British Guardian](https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/jan/11/china-mystery-illness-outbreak-causes-first-death): According to the official announcement of Wuhan, a 61-year-old The infected person died, and 41 people were diagnosed, 2 were cured, and 739 people were reported to have contact with the diagnosed patients. <br>

## January 12, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
* In the morning, [The Third Session of the 13th People ’s Congress of Hubei Province](http://www.hubei.gov.cn/zwgk/hbyw/hbywqb/202001/t20200113_1910934.shtml) was grandly opened in Hongshan Auditorium, Wuchang. Jiang Chaoliang, Ma Guoqiang, Wang Ruilian, Wang Ling, Zhou Hongyu, Wang Jianming, Liu Xuerong, Liu Xiaoming, Hu Zhiqiang, and Wang Yaping took seats in the front row of the rostrum. The opening meeting was chaired by Jiang Chaoliang. <br>
* In the morning, Director Xu of the Law Enforcement and Supervision Department of the Hubei Provincial Health and Health Commission led a team to the Houhu District of Wuhan Central Hospital to supervise and issue hot-related consultations, instructing that the report card for infectious diseases should be reported carefully, and the province and the city shall jointly determine the report card. [Refer to January 4th and 5th] See March 5th [Freezing Point Weekly:Why the early epidemic report in Wuhan was interrupted](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/148#issue-577265152) Provide ["Outbreak Disposal Information"](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/149#issue-577432227). <br>
* A three-member expert team from the Wuhan Municipal Health and Health Commission went to Zhongnan Hospital for investigation. According to Peng Zhiyong, director of the Department of Critical Care Medicine, "The expert group said that clinical manifestations and SARS are indeed a bit similar, but they are still talking about the diagnostic criteria. We have reflected that the diagnostic criteria are too harsh. According to this standard, it is difficult for someone to Will be diagnosed "," Previously, a team of experts appointed by the National Health and Health Commission went to Jinyintan Hospital to conduct an investigation and made a set of diagnostic criteria. There should be a history of exposure to the seafood market in South China, fever symptoms, and a positive virus test. These three The diagnosis can only be confirmed if the standards are met. Especially the third point is very harsh. In fact, very few people can do virus detection. " At this time, Peng Zhiyong knew that other hospitals were also reporting to the Wuhan Health and Health Commission. See February 5th [Caixin.com:Critical Physician: How we rescue critical patients](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/IlQyOfQtsyvpptPAlTjwPg). [According to what Peng Zhiyong said "before", it refers to the second group of experts who arrived in Wuhan on January 8 for investigation, not the first group on December 31, because there was no virus detection at that time. 】 In addition, according to the article “New Coronary Pneumonia, the Node of the Hospital”, the 7th issue of “Sanlian Life Weekly” in 2020, in addition to the above three items, the diagnosis criteria are “invalid antiviral therapy for three days”. However, on January 9, Xu Jianguo has publicly indicated to the media that this unexplained viral pneumonia pathogen was initially determined to be a new coronavirus. Peng Zhiyong recalled, "Since it is viral pneumonia, it should not be treated with antibiotics." At that time, the power of testing reagents was controlled by the Hubei Provincial Center for Disease Control. At that time, only one institution could do reagent testing and make the final diagnosis of unknown pneumonia. See "Sanlian Life Weekly" 2020 No. 7 [New Coronary Pneumonia, Hospital Node](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/138). <br>
* Wuhan City CDC began to issue documents and forms to major hospitals, requesting hospitals to report fever in outpatient clinics. At first, it was required to report before 4 pm every day, but it was gradually changed to 8-10 pm at night. See February 11 [Eight o'clock Jianwen:Lost Opportunity, Case of Small Hospital Early Neglected in New Crown Outbreak](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/91). <br>

## January 13, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
* In the early morning, the Wuhan Municipal Health Commission issued the [Sixth Announcement](http://wjw.wuhan.gov.cn/front/web/showDetail/2020011309038), indicating that as of 24 o’clock on the 12th, "no new crown One case of pneumonia infected by the virus was cured and discharged, and no new deaths were reported. " [China CDC](http://www.chinacdc.cn/jkzt/crb/zl/szkb_11803/jszl_11809/202001/t20200119_211277.html) full text reprint announcement. <br>
* At 9 o'clock in the morning, Wu Fengbo, director of the Department of Disease Control and Prevention of the Wuhan Municipal Health Commission, and the staff of the Department of Disease Control and Prevention of the District Health and Health Commission, went to the Nanjing Road Campus of Wuhan Central Hospital to convey the latest report of unexplained pneumonia cases. The director pointed out that cases of unexplained pneumonia should be reported carefully. The found cases of viral pneumonia must first complete all inspections and related examinations in the hospital. After consultation by the expert team in the hospital for unexplained pneumonia, they should report to the district health committee and inform the district disease control sampling. After the district, city, province Level-by-level testing, after still unexplained pneumonia, can only report the case information "with the consent of the Provincial Health Commission". Another document from the public health department of the hospital recorded the details of the communication activities that day, which mentioned the reporting of unexplained pneumonia cases in other hospitals-as of January 13, Wuhan Union Hospital reported a total of 11 cases , Hubei Province Integrated Traditional Chinese and Western Medicine Hospital reported 9 cases. According to Lu Yi (pseudonym), a doctor at Wuhan Central Hospital, this requirement of "reporting caution" has evolved into "not reporting as much as possible" in Wuhan Central Hospital. See March 5th [Freezing Point Weekly:Why Wuhan Early Epidemic Reporting Was Suspended Once](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/148#issue-577265152) to provide ["Description of Epidemic Disposal Situation"]( https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/149#issue-577432227) and March 16 [Global Times:Wuhan Central Hospital Medical staff vomiting the truth: the epidemic is a face mirror] [https: // github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/167#issue-583545656). <br>
* At 9 o'clock, a doctor from the Public Health Department of Wuhan Central Hospital received a call from Wang Wenyong, chief of the Department of Prevention and Control of the Jianghan District Disease Control Center, and was asked to revise the unexplained pneumonia cases reported on the 10th to other diseases. See a doctor from the Public Health Department of Wuhan Central Hospital on February 8 ["Description of Outbreak Disposal"](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/149#issue-577432227). <br>

" At the same time, it was pointed out that "Thailand notified and diagnosed a case of pneumonia caused by a new coronavirus infection in Wuhan City. It is currently isolated and treated in Thailand, and its close contacts who are returning to China are carrying out follow-up medical observation." All localities are required to attach great importance to "stress politics and take into account the overall situation", take epidemic prevention and control as the top priority of the current health system, and demand "strengthen information sharing and joint prevention and control within the system, between departments, and between regions" at the meeting. See January 22 [National News Office holds a press conference on the prevention and control of pneumonia caused by new coronavirus infection](http://www.scio.gov.cn/xwfbh/xwbfbh/wqfbh/42311/42470/index.htm) , The official website of the National Health and Health Commission for February and March 5 [Freezing Point Weekly:Why the early epidemic report in Wuhan was interrupted](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/148#issue-577265152). [According to, according to the author of the WeChat article "Wuhan Dumping Conference Fourth Round Opening" on March 9th, the notice of the National Health and Health Commission's "Deployment of New Coronavirus Infection Pneumonia Prevention and Control Work held by the National Health and Health Commission held a national video and telephone conference" is February On the website, the publication time is on a day before February 21st, and the last modification time is 8:39 a.m. on February 21st, then the article's publication time is adjusted to January 14th. 】 <br>
* IJID published in the International Journal of Infectious Diseases [about the continuing impact of the 2019-nCoV epidemic on international health](https://www.ijidonline.com/article/S1201-9712(20)30011-4/fulltext) After the China Health and Health Commission notified the International Health Organization of the new coronavirus, the health authorities in Hong Kong, Macau, and Taiwan stepped up border inspections and feared that the new virus would threaten international public health. As of January 10, 41 patients had been infected with the new coronavirus with symptoms of fever (> 90%), diarrhea, dry cough (80%), shortness of breath (20%), and dyspnea (15%). Although there have been no new cases in Wuhan since January 3, the first case in Thailand was discovered on January 13. The case has never had direct contact with the South China Seafood Market. <br>
* [British Guardian](https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/jan/14/case-of-mystery-coronavirus-found-outside-china-for-the-first-time-thailand): According to the Thai official announcement, the first confirmed case of new pneumonia in Wuhan was found outside of China. The woman developed the disease on January 5 local time and was taken to the hospital on January 8. Contacted a farmer's market in Wuhan, but the market was not officially identified as a source of infection by Wuhan officials. <br>

Employees of the seafood wholesale market, his wife denied having a history of exposure to the seafood wholesale market in South China, "and" no community transmission has been found so far. " [Chinese Center for Disease Control](http://www.chinacdc.cn/jkzt/crb/zl/szkb_11803/jszl_11809/202001/t20200119_211280.html) This knowledge question and answer is reproduced in full text. * The Hubei Provincial Health and Health Commission requires Tongji Hospital, Provincial People's Hospital and Union Hospital to take over the 7th, 6th and 5th floors of Jinyintan Hospital respectively. The three-story building was subsequently transformed into a severe ICU ward, and municipal hospitals were deployed to support them. * Between January 12 and 15, one day, Jinyintan Hospital suddenly left more than 50 health workers. They were so scared to see that patients came so much and the medical staff were so tightly protected. Although Jinyintan Hospital also requires health workers to have all three levels of protection, just like their own employees, because they will pollute our colleagues, but some people are still very scared. There are more than 100 health workers in Jinyintan Hospital, half of them. There were also 18 security guards hired temporarily at that time, but one day all of them suddenly stopped coming. See March 17 [Voice of China:[Oral Record] Zhang Dingyu: I am in the Eye of the Storm ｜ Wuhan Wuhan](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/168#issue-583557307) Zhang Dingyu recalled . <br>

Since there are no new cases of infection in the Mainland after 3 days, it can be judged that the epidemic has been controlled. Even if it is passed from person to person, it is very limited. <br>
* On the same day, Hong Kong reporters visiting with Hong Kong experts were intercepted during the shooting in the hospital area, and then taken to the police station in the hospital. Radio and commercial radio stations, TVB, NOW News reporters and photographers were also taken to The same police station. <br>
* According to a Hong Kong expert delegation visiting Wuhan on the 13th, there were two groups of family infections among Wuhan pneumonia patients. In addition to the group notified by the Wuhan Health and Health Commission, there was also a group of "patients who were a pair of father and son and nephew". The three of them were operating stores in South China Seafood City together. The time of onset was very close. It was possible that they were jointly exposed to the source of infection rather than being transmitted from person to person. " See January 15 [Caixin.com:Hong Kong: Wuhan pneumonia patients are mostly aquatic vendors in the South China Seafood Market](http://www.caixin.com/2020-01-15/101504503.html). <br>

In addition, WHO has issued guidelines for epidemic prevention to hospitals worldwide. <br>

## January 16, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
* In the early morning, the Wuhan Municipal Health Commission issued the [Ninth Announcement](http://wjw.wuhan.gov.cn/front/web/showDetail/2020011609057), indicating that as of 24 o’clock on the 15th, "no new crown Viral infection of pneumonia cases, 5 cases were cured and discharged, and 1 new death case (Xiong, 69 years old) "," 119 people are still under medical observation, and no related cases have been found in close contacts ". <br>

See January 19 [Xinhua News Agency:Epidemic can be prevented and controlled-Wuhan City responds to reporters' questions regarding comprehensive prevention and control of pneumonia caused by new coronavirus infection](http://www.xinhuanet.com//2020-01/19 /c_1125480602.htm) Huang Chaolin of Wuhan Electric made a speech. On the 14th, I went to the hospital to understand the clinical manifestations of the patients and the measures for the control of severe negative pressure isolation wards. They found that in 41 cases, there were 2 family gatherings, one was a husband and wife (the wife had not been to the market, and the onset time was 5 days after the husband, and it was difficult for a limited person to pass from person to person). The other was a father, son, and nephew (All work in the market, and the onset date is within 2 days, may be due to exposure to some unexplained infection source).

In the afternoon, the Spring Festival Gala in the hospital was cancelled and the isolation ward was started. At this time, a large number of suspected cases in the hospital were not reported because they did not meet the standards for reporting the exposure history and fever of the South China market set by the expert team of the National Health and Health Commission. See February 11 [Eight o'clock Jianwen:Lost Opportunity, Case of Small Hospital Early Neglected in New Crown Outbreak](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/91). <br>

Youfu Hospital began to report a large number of cases to the disease control department, and reported 30 fever patients at once. The previous epidemic was more complete In the review, Zheng Ziyu (pseudonym), one of the earliest patients mentioned, started to have a fever on December 12, 2019 and experienced two transfers. Based on the article that some patients have not been to the South China Seafood Wholesale Market, they have vaguely expressed their concern about the possibility of person-to-person transmission [see entry on December 12]. <br>

【China】 <br>
* Yuan Guoyong, a member of the high-level expert group of the National Health and Health Commission, previously discovered a family aggregation case that returned from Wuhan to Shenzhen. One of the patients who had no history of Wuhan travel was also tested positive by the new coronavirus nucleic acid, so he believed that the new coronavirus pneumonia Can spread among people. On January 17, he notified this fact to Gao Fu, director of the Chinese Center for Disease Control and Guangdong Center for Disease Control through a written report, and disclosed this information to other panelists. On the morning of the same day, the leaders of Guangdong Province and Academician Zhong Nanshan led a team to Shenzhen to investigate the epidemic prevention and control. See [Jasper Fuk-Woo Chan, et. A familial cluster of pneumonia associated with the 2019 novel coronavirus indicating person-to-person transmission: a study of a family cluster. The Lancet, Jan. 24, 2020 (and the 2019 new crown A virus-associated case of family cluster pneumonia indicates the spread of the virus from person to person: a study of family cluster cases)](https://www.thelancet.com/journals/lancet/article/PIIS0140-6736(20)30154- 9 / fulltext), January 27 [Financial Magazine:Expert Committee of National Health and Health Commission Yuan Guoyong: "Wuhan pneumonia" still needs to determine a more accurate fatality rate](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/mrulHdV7HwSi2ImuEzYfng ) And February 25 [Southern Metropolis Daily:Details disclosed! Guangdong's first "onset" family confirmed the diagnosis process](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/ry0Mo5coz_zszsOJJuKylA). <br>
* The National Health and Safety Commission has dispatched 7 supervision groups to supervise and inspect 8 provinces including Hebei and Guangdong to guide prevention and control work. See January 22 [The State Council Office holds a press conference on the prevention and control of pneumonia caused by new coronavirus infection] Li Bin spoke. <br>

## January 18, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
* In the early morning, the Wuhan Municipal Health Commission issued the [Tenth Announcement](http://wjw.wuhan.gov.cn/front/web/showDetail/2020011809064), indicating that as of 16 o'clock on the 16th, 3 patients were cured and discharged. "New death cases", "4 new cases of pneumonia infected by new coronavirus" in our city, "the new cases have been transferred to the Jinyintan Hospital in Wuhan City for treatment. All cases are in stable condition and there is no critical illness. The incidence of cases is concentrated in January 5-8 ". [China Center for Disease Control](http://www.chinacdc.cn/jkzt/crb/zl/szkb_11803/jszl_11809/202001/t20200118_211269.html) was reprinted in full the day before. <br>
* The second expert group appointed by the National Health and Welfare Institute visited the four major hospitals including Wuhan University Central South Hospital and People's Hospital. Peng Zhiyong of Zhongnan Hospital reported that the previous diagnosis standard was set too high, so it is easy to miss the real patient. "This is an infectious disease, and the diagnosis criteria are tightened too much, and letting out the sick people is very harmful to society. After the second expert group of the National Health and Health Commission came, the diagnosis criteria changed and the number of diagnosed patients increased dramatically ". See February 5 [Caixin.com:Critical Physician: How we rescue critical patients](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/IlQyOfQtsyvpptPAlTjwPg). During the investigation by the expert group, the four major hospitals also reported the infection of medical staff, and again put forward the requirement to reduce the diagnostic criteria of suspected cases. At the same time, the report form issued to the hospital by the disease control department has added an infection case for medical staff. See February 11 [Eight o'clock Jianwen:Lost Opportunity, Case of Small Hospital Early Neglected in New Crown Outbreak](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/91). <br>
* On the same day, the Baibuting Garden Community in Jiang'an District, Wuhan City held a family banquet, and more than 40,000 families spent the Lunar New Year together. Regarding whether it was inappropriate for large-scale personnel to gather together under the Wuhan pneumonia epidemic, the staff responded to a reporter from the Beijing News that “we have all taken appropriate measures”. See January 21st [New Beijing News:A community in Wuhan holds a 10,000 family banquet, and the person in charge of the community: everything is normal](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/2#issue-556730991). <br>

【China】 <br>
* In the afternoon, Academician Zhong Nanshan, who had just returned from Shenzhen to Guangzhou, received a notice from his superior requesting him to go to Wuhan immediately, and then formed a high-level expert group of the National Health and Health Commission with other experts, and arrived in Wuhan that night. See January 21 [Guangzhou Daily:84-year-old Zhong Nanshan, fight the epidemic front again! These two photos are awe-inspiring! ](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/dOfUWIwnYhGIm9eH7atbyQ). <br>

【International】 <br>
* On the same day, [Thailand and Japan notifications](http://wjw.wuhan.gov.cn/front/web/showDetail/2020011809065) diagnosed a case of pneumonia from a new coronavirus infection in Wuhan. Diagnosed cases in Thailand are being treated in hospital, and close contacts are observed; cases diagnosed in Japan have been discharged. <br>
* [Singapore Lianhe Zaobao](http://www.zaobao.com/special/report/politic/hkpol/story20200118-1022055) reported, "Because Wuhan ’s new pneumonia epidemic shows signs of spread, the Hong Kong SAR Government has decided to expand the scope of surveillance Those who have visited hospitals in mainland China or have been in close contact with patients diagnosed with new coronavirus will be included in the reporting mechanism. "<br>
* [British Guardian](https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/jan/17/corona-second-death-in-china-after-sars-like-outbreak): the first of the new coronavirus pneumonia Two deaths were confirmed by Chinese officials.
* [British Guardian](https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/jan/18/coronavirus-what-airport-measures-are-in-place-to-detect-for-sick-passengers): Three US airports (Los Angeles International Airport, San Francisco International Airport and New York ’s JFK International Airport) have set up temperature monitoring facilities for passengers from Wuhan, and passengers will be monitored for signs of new coronavirus pneumonia. <br>

" "Using the optimized detection kit, it is proposed that" we will continue to expand the search scope, identify suspected cases, and carry out sampling and testing. "[CCTV News Weibo](https://weibo.com/2656274875/Iq7jtiXv2) Full text reprinted. * In the early morning, the Wuhan Municipal Health and Health Commission held a press conference to answer reporters' questions regarding the comprehensive prevention and control of pneumonia caused by new coronavirus infection in Wuhan. Li Gang, director of the Wuhan Center for Disease Control and Prevention, said: "The initial impression of this epidemic is that the new coronavirus is not very contagious. It does not rule out the possibility of limited person-to-person transmission, but the risk of continued person-to-person transmission is low. With the various prevention and control The implementation and implementation of measures, the epidemic situation is preventable and controllable. " The Vice Mayor of Wuhan Municipal People's Government Chen Yongxin and Huang Jinlin, Vice President of Wuhan Jinyintan Hospital also attended the press conference. In addition, it is worth noting that Huang Chaolin had already felt strange on January 17, and was diagnosed as a new coronary pneumonia patient by nucleic acid detection on January 22, but none of the three men wore masks at the press conference at the time. The leaders of the National Health Commission attached great importance and immediately reported to the relevant leaders of the State Council. As soon as the meeting was over, members of the high-level expert group returned to Beijing overnight. <br>

## January 20, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
* At 2 a.m., the Wuhan Municipal Health Commission issued the [Twelfth Announcement](http://wjw.wuhan.gov.cn/front/web/showDetail/2020012009077), indicating that the cumulative number of newly diagnosed cases on the 18th and 19th 136 Cases, including 100 cases of mild, 33 cases of severe, and 3 cases of critical illness (including 1 death). 170 cases are still being treated in the hospital, including 126 cases of mild, 35 cases of severe, and 9 cases of critically ill, all received isolation treatment at designated medical institutions in Wuhan. 727 people have been dismissed from medical observation and 90 people are still undergoing medical observation. Among close contacts, no related cases have been found. [China CDC](http://www.chinacdc.cn/jkzt/crb/zl/szkb_11803/jszl_11809/202001/t20200120_211298.html) full text reprint announcement. <br>
* On the same day, Director Lu Xiaohong of the Gastroenterology Department of the Fifth Hospital of Wuhan City sent a text message to the principal of the nearby high school to leave the senior high school students who had planned to make up classes. See [Freezing Weekly:Before Zhong Nanshan ’s speech, the doctor in Wuhan issued an outbreak alert to nearby schools](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/39#issue-558504017) <br>
* On the same day, with the consent of the Chinese government, the World Health Organization sent a group of five-member delegation led by WHO Representative in China to Dr. Gauden Galea to Wuhan for a two-day inspection (January 20 -21). During the visit, the delegation visited Wuhan Tianhe International Airport, Central South Hospital and Hubei Provincial Centers for Disease Control and Prevention, including the BSL3 laboratory of the Chinese Center for Disease Control (CDC), to confirm the transmission of human-to-human and medical personnel in the epidemic. According to Peng Zhiyong, director of the Department of Intensive Medicine of Zhongnan Hospital, the expert team visited his ward that day and was shocked, "You are all patients here, don't you mean that you have only two people in the intensive care unit?" See January 22 [World Health Organization:Wuhan Summary of the inspection report: WHO conducts an on-site inspection in Wuhan, China, January 20-21, 2020](https://www.who.int/china/zh/news/detail/22-01-2020-field-visit -wuhan-china-jan-2020), January 23 [AP:Q & A: WHO representative addresses China's new virus outbreak](https://apnews.com/0e46df9113bd32507d08c1e0569a814e) and Sanlian Life Weekly Issue No. 7 in 2020 [ New Coronary Pneumonia, the node of the hospital](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/138). <br>
* At 19 o'clock, [Wuhan City Health and Health Commission](http://wjw.wuhan.gov.cn/front/web/showDetail/2020012009078) announced the list of popular medical institutions and designated medical institutions. <br>
* In the evening, the Emergency Management Department of Hubei Province successfully held the Spring Festival Gala of "Immering the Harvest with Sweat and Working Hard to Move Forward". <br>

【China】 <br>
* At 8:30, the high-level expert group came to Zhongnanhai. Vice Premier Sun Chunlan listened in detail to everyone's report on the epidemic situation judgment. She attached great importance to the expert group's opinions. See March 27 [Chinese Journal of Health · [Interview with Zhongwei] Li Fengjuan is on the verge of release, Li Lanjuan first disclosed details of the closure of Wuhan](https://www.thepaper.cn/newsDetail_forward_6715744). <br>
* At 10 o'clock, [CCTV News Weibo](https://weibo.com/2656274875/IqkydFW0z) reported that Zhejiang had found 5 patients with fever and respiratory symptoms from Wuhan to Zhejiang. <br>
* In the morning, Premier Li Keqiang of the State Council presided over an executive meeting of the State Council, which specifically added a new type of coronavirus infection prevention and control of pneumonia, and Zhong Nanshan and Li Lanjuan also attended. Based on Li Lanjuan ’s suggestion, the meeting decided to include the new coronavirus-infected pneumonia in the category B infectious diseases as stipulated in the “Law of the People ’s Republic of China on the Prevention and Control of Infectious Diseases”, and adopt prevention and control measures for category A infectious diseases. She also suggested that Wuhan should take "no entry and no exit" measures. See [Announcement of National Health and Health Commission] on January 20 (http://www.nhc.gov.cn/jkj/s7916/202001/44a3b8245e8049d2837a4f27529cd386.shtml), January 23 [Qianjiang Evening News · Hour News:Li Lanjuan: Yesterday it was proposed to close the city of Wuhan, and the state took action today](https://www.thehour.cn/news/339129.html), February 20 [Xinhuanet:Chinese Academy of Infectious Diseases Li Lanjuan: Fight with everyone](http://www.zj.xinhuanet.com/2020-02/20/c_1125601526.htm) and March 27 [Chinese Journal of Health · [Interview with Zhongwei] Unblocking soon, Li Lanjuan first discloses details of the closure of Wuhan]( https://www.thepaper.cn/newsDetail_forward_6715744). <br>
* In the afternoon, the State Council and the National Health Commission held a national video and telephone conference, and Vice Premier Sun Chunlan laid out the requirements for national joint defense and joint control. In the evening, a meeting was convened to study and deploy prevention and control work. See January 22 [The State Council Office holds a press conference on the prevention and control of pneumonia caused by new coronavirus infection] Li Bin's speech and March 27 [Chinese Journal of Health · [Interview with Zhongwei] Li Fengjuan is on the verge of release, Li Lanjuan first discloses details of the closure of Wuhan](https://www.thepaper.cn/newsDetail_forward_6715744). <br>
* At the same time, in response to the prevention and control of the "new coronavirus-infected pneumonia epidemic", Academician Zhong Nanshan, head of the high-level expert group of the National Health and Health Commission, Gao Fu, Li Lanjuan, Yuan Guoyong, and Zeng Guang, members of the high-level expert group of the National Health and Health Commission Answered questions from reporters on issues of public concern. During the period, Zhong Nanshan confirmed the spread of human-to-human transmission and infection by medical personnel, but the news was not immediately disclosed. See January 20 [CCTV News:High-level expert group of the National Health and Health Commission answers reporters' questions about new coronavirus pneumonia](http://m.news.cctv.com/2020/01/20/ARTIF4Fl7LEu8TRqIsnde93B200120.shtml). <br>
* At 19 o'clock, "News Network" reported Xinhua News Agency, the State Council issued [Xi Jinping made important instructions on the pneumonia epidemic of new coronavirus infection](http://www.gov.cn/xinwen/2020-01/20/content_5471057. htm). <br>
* In the evening, CCTV News [News 1 + 1](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/3#issue-556734943) Bai Yansong interviewed Academician Zhong Nanshan on-site, confirming that the new coronavirus can be passed from person to person, And the medical staff has been infected. <br>
* On the same day, Wang Guangfa's new crown virus nucleic acid test was positive, and lung CT showed typical pneumonia. New crown pneumonia was diagnosed in Beijing. See February 2 [Bingdian Weekly:Wang Guang, a member of the Expert Committee of the Health and Welfare Committee, was issued to the hospital and answered our 8 questions](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/DWcRVz10zps27VIrml_Khg) <br>

## January 22, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
* In the early morning, the Hubei Provincial Government launched a Class II emergency response to public health emergencies and issued a notice to the whole province. <br>
* At 9 o'clock, merchants in the South China Seafood Market wear masks and gather in long queues to lead the rent refund. <br>
* In the morning, the Health and Health Commission of Jianghan District, Wuhan City informed that each community health service center would send two doctors and one nurse to support the designated hospital (the list of the first seven designated hospitals at that time was just confirmed). According to the relevant provisions of the "Law of the People's Republic of China on the Prevention and Control of Infectious Diseases", the province's new coronavirus infection caused by pneumonia is issued by the provincial health department. <br>
* In the evening, the Hubei Provincial Health Commission held the first [news coronavirus infection pneumonia prevention and control work press conference](http://wjw.hubei.gov.cn/fbjd/dtyw/202001/t20200130_2016538.shtml), "As of January 22 at 20 o'clock, Hubei Province has reported a total of 444 cases of new coronavirus-infected pneumonia (from 0:00 to 20 o'clock on January 22, Hubei Province added 69 cases of new coronavirus-infected pneumonia, of which Wuhan There were 62 new cases in the city and 8 deaths; 6 new cases in Jingzhou City and 1 new case in Jingmen City). 28 cases were cured and discharged, and 17 cases died. " And near the 7 large hospitals in the city, 7 secondary public hospitals were selected as the designated hospitals for hot clinics, transferring patients and vacating wards, all of which were used to receive fever patients. <br>
* On the same day, Huang Chaolin's nucleic acid test was positive, confirming the diagnosis of new coronary pneumonia. There are ground glass-like lesions in both lungs. More people may come back in the future , Will cause a greater spread of the epidemic. Li Lanjuan once again urgently suggested to the country that Wuhan must strictly "close the city". Explain that you may be at Jinyintan Hospital in Wuhan, or you may have gone to a fever clinic and temporarily isolated wards in several hospitals two days before returning to Beijing. <br>

## January 23, 2020, 29
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
* In the early morning, Wuhan released the news "Fengcheng". At 10 o'clock, the Lihan Channel was closed, but private reports are still available at high speed. <br>
* The materials of the whole hospital of Wuhan Central Hospital are in an emergency. Everyone went to ask for help in their own name. They were blocked by the hospital and no private fundraising was allowed. See March 11 [Southern Weekend · Four people killed, four people are in danger-Wuhan Central Hospital "to the dark"] Yang Er (pseudonym), a front-line doctor at the hospital, recalled. At the same time, some medical professionals began to urgently ask for material support for 10 local hospitals such as Wuhan Concord on Weibo. <br>
* At 17:00, the Wuhan Municipal Health and Fitness Commission issued ["Answers on Several Issues Concerned by the Citizen"](http://wjw.wuhan.gov.cn/front/web/showDetail/2020012309114), replying to "Sample Case The detection process is as follows: the first-diagnosis hospital passes the standardized pre-examination triage, combined with clinical examination, laboratory examination and chest imaging examination, after the expert group consultation, the suspected case is confirmed and sampled, and the sample is transferred to the city The CDC and the Municipal CDC transported to the provincial CDC for nucleic acid testing, which can detect more than 200 samples per day ", and admitted that" there is no kit in our province before January 16 and needs to be sent to a nationally designated testing agency " Carry out virus isolation and nucleic acid testing "," Samples need to be sent to a designated testing institution in Beijing, and the results will be returned in about 3-5 days. " <br>
* The Hubei Provincial Health and Health Commission held a [news coronavirus infection pneumonia epidemic prevention and control work press conference (second session)](http://wjw.hubei.gov.cn/fbjd/dtyw/202001/t20200130_2016539.shtml) . <br>
* In the evening, the Wuhan Red Cross Hospital, which treats fever patients at designated locations, was just opened. More than 2,000 people crowded the hospital. A tent was set up outside, and many fever patients in Jianghan District were led there. Even if it is ordinary fever, residents must go to the hospital to find out whether it is the new crown virus. Usually, the hospital's ability to receive consultations is just a few hundred people, which greatly exceeds the hospital's ability to operate. The hospital is full of corridors where no garbage is collected, and some people fall in line. See March 7 [Eight o'clock news:Wuhan's first line of defense-how did the community health service center fail? ](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/150#issue-577432320) Fang Han, Dean of a community health service center in Jianghan District, recalled. <br>
* At 21:00, ["Chutian Metropolis Daily"](https://weibo.com/2656274875/IqVg4toO2) reported that Wuhan, Hubei, will build an emergency hospital in the "Xiaotangshan" mode, with a construction area of ​​25,000 square meters, which can accommodate With 1000 beds, the hospital will be built in 6 days. <br>
* Hubei Governor Wang Xiaodong was interviewed by [CCTV](https://weibo.com/2656274875/IqRSLEnXs) on the first day of the closure of the city, saying that “despite the market volatility, Wuhan ’s reserves and market supply are sufficient.” <br>

It is conservatively estimated that Wuhan has more pneumonia infections than SARS. "" The local health protection has not been upgraded at all "and I feel that I have missed the gold prevention and control. In the future, the effect of the closure was not optimistic. <br>
* [Hong Kong Cable News](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ACwLJ_NduOg) interviewed some senior citizens of the Guangzhou Flower Market, they said they were “surprised by the government”, “trusted the government” and “no masks”. Afterwards, it was made into an expression package by netizens and circulated. <br>

* The seven cities of Hubei are closed. <br>

At present, 494 cases are still being treated in the hospital, including 106 severe cases and critical illnesses. 23 cases, all received isolation treatment in designated medical institutions. " <br>

The subjects he interviewed included doctors, nurses, volunteers, ordinary residents, patients and family members of victims. <br>

Yang Gonghuan, the former deputy director of the Chinese Center for Disease Control and Prevention, said that he had consulted relevant CDC personnel and learned that he had not received "direct reports" of unexplained pneumonia cases in December last year. "They said that they received information from Wuhan from January 3 to January 10, but then they suddenly stopped. They did not resume reporting until January 24 when the new coronary pneumonia was added to the network direct reporting system. "See March 5 [Freezing Point Weekly:Why was the early epidemic report in Wuhan interrupted](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/148#issue-577265152). <br>

【International】 <br>
* On the same day, [two cases of pneumonia diagnosed with new coronavirus infection were confirmed in France](https://news.sina.com.cn/o/2020-01-25/doc-iihnzahk6215027.shtml), which is also the first new type of diagnosis in Europe Pneumonia cases of coronavirus infection.
* The top international medical journal The Lancet ("Lancet") published [Clinical features of patients infected with 2019 novel coronavirus in Wuhan, China ("Clinical features of patients with 2019 new coronavirus infection in clinical features of Wuhan")](https: //github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/26#issue-557972097). The article recorded and analyzed the clinical data of 41 cases in the initial stage of the epidemic. The article showed that the first known symptomatic case (December 1, confirmed afterwards) did not contact the South China Seafood Wholesale Market. (For more information, see the previous article) The first case related to Seafood City appeared on December 10. The first author of the article is Huang Chaolin, vice president of Wuhan Jinyintan Hospital. Other authors include Li Xingwang, Wang Guangfa (second batch) and Jiang Rongmeng, members of the National Expert Group. Cao Bin, Beijing-China Friendship Hospital, and Wang Jianwei, Peking Union Medical College Hospital are co-corresponding authors.
* On the same day, "The Lancet" was published as [2019 familial cluster of pneumonia associated with the 2019 novel coronavirus indicating person-to-person transmission: a study of a family cluster)](https: / /github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/28) article, confirming that a virus infects a family, the virus gene sequence is different (meaning that the virus has different degrees of variation in different human bodies), and the virus is in the virus library Coronavirus has never been seen before (the virus structure is not yet understood). <br>
* [Singapore Lianhe Zaobao](http://www.zaobao.com/znews/international/story20200124-1023619): British experts warn that there are at least 4,000 people, and the worst case in Wuhan is that nearly 10,000 people get sick. <br>
* Zhu ​​Na and others from the Chinese New Coronavirus Research Group published in the NEJM "New England Medical Journal" [A Novel Coronavirus from Patients with Pneumonia in China, 2019 ("New Coronavirus Isolated from Chinese Pneumonia Patients in 2019")](https://www.nejmqianyan.cn/article/YXQYoa2001017), an article reported that a new coronavirus was isolated from the airway epithelial cells of three cases who had contact with the South China seafood market and named 2019- nCov. The new virus belongs to the genus β-coronavirus and is commonly found in humans, bats, and other wild animals. Information about the virus update has been obtained from 830 patients.

## Tuesday, January 26, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
* Hubei Provincial Health and Health Commission held [New Coronavirus Infection Pneumonia Outbreak Prevention and Control Work Press Conference (Fifth Session)](http://wjw.hubei.gov.cn/fbjd/dtyw/202001/t20200130_2016542.shtml) , Hubei Governor Wang Xiaodong, Wuhan Mayor Zhou Xianwang, and Provincial Government Secretary-General Bi Bixiong presided over, the mayor said, "As of yesterday at 24 o'clock, that is, early this morning, the cumulative number of new coronavirus infections of pneumonia was 618 40 cases have been cured and discharged, and 45 cases have died. At present, 533 cases are treated in the hospital, including 87 severe cases and 53 critical cases. These are all treated in isolation in designated hospitals in Wuhan. " <br>
* Sichuan Medical Assistance Team for Hubei entered the Wuhan Red Cross Hospital. According to Huang Xiaobo, the Sichuan Provincial People's Hospital who accompanied the team, only 10 virus samples were tested in the hospital on that day, and there were hundreds of hot clinics and more than 300 inpatients. See February 10 [Caixin.cn:Cover report:The directors of the four major ICU explained the prevention and control strategies of the virus from the frontline](http://weekly.caixin.com/2020-02-07/101512870_all.html#page2) . <br>
* Wuhan Central Hospital used to "cut grain". There are usually 2,000 people in the canteen and two meals a day. In extraordinary times, medical staff and patients are living in the hospital, and three meals a day are used to prepare meals for 6,000 people. Many medical staff insisted on snacking that day, and some departments "cut food" for one day, and some for three days. See March 11 [Southern Weekend · Four people killed, four are endangered-"the darkest moment" of Wuhan Central Hospital]]. <br>

【China】 <br>
* The National Health and Health Commission released the new coronavirus-infected pneumonia situation [Sixth Announcement](http://www.nhc.gov.cn/xcs/yqtb/202001/9614b05a8cac4ffabac10c4502fe517c.shtml), as of January 25, 24 At that time, a total of 1975 confirmed cases were reported in China, and 1 new case was confirmed in Australia. <br>
* The National Health and Health Commission Grassroots Health Department issued [About
Notice on Strengthening the Prevention and Control of Pneumonia Epidemic Infected by New Coronavirus in Primary Medical and Health Institutions] In community outbreak areas, community health service centers should assist in tracking and managing close contacts of confirmed cases and suspected cases, cooperate with higher-level disease control agencies to conduct standard case epidemiological investigations, and assist in implementing home medical observation measures for close contacts. Prior to this, the Wuhan-Hubei community health service center had been absent. See March 7 [Eight o'clock news:Wuhan's first line of defense-how did the community health service center fail? ]. <br>
* The National Center for Disease Control successfully isolated the virus and began to develop vaccines. <br>
* In the epidemic situation conference of the State Council of China, Wuhan issued a list of needs to the Ministry of Industry and Information Technology, requiring 100,000 sets of medical protective clothing every day and 3 million sets a month. Now stocks and reserves are used, and there is a great contradiction between supply and demand. There are about 40 manufacturers distributed in 14 provinces and cities across the country, and now the production capacity has recovered by about 40%, and it can supply 13,000 pieces per day, which is far from enough. The export production capacity is 50,000 pieces per day, but there is a problem with the docking with the national standard, and it is still docking with CE and US standards. There are still 220,000 pieces purchased overseas (purchased, the arrival is not clear). Since then, hospitals in Wuhan and Hubei have begun to collect medical supplies from all walks of life. According to statistics from the medical website Dingyuan, as of January 29, nearly 136 hospitals in Hubei Province have released information on the application of medical supplies. <br>
* At 14 o'clock, Guangdong issued a strict [epidemic prevention notice](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzA5NDM2OTkwOA==&mid=2655627252&idx=1&sn=530ab731f325f7916eb832e68f0b92aa), and no masks will be punished in public places. <br>
* [Announced by the Hong Kong Special Administrative Region Government](https://www.info.gov.hk/gia/general/202001/26/P2020012600713.htm) Effective January 27, except for Hong Kong residents, residents of Hubei Province and any People who have visited Hubei Province in the past 14 days entered Hong Kong.

## January 27th, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>

Disclosure, as a local government, after I obtained the information, I could only disclose it after authorization. This was not understood at that time. <br>

Ma Guoqiang, deputy secretary of the Hubei Provincial Party Committee and secretary of the Wuhan Municipal Party Committee, pointed out that all donated materials must go through the Red Cross. <br>
* [Wu Ming, Director of Wuhan ICU](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/43#issue-558509418) said that because he was busy treating critically ill patients, he often had to be busy until two or three in the morning With a bite of rice, you can only rest for two or three hours a day. Peers cover their heads with file bags and shoes with garbage bags. The patient lived in a ward in one hour, and it was not necessary to queue up at the hospital due to panic. <br>

【China】 <br>
* Early morning news, [Xinhua News Agency](http://www.xinhuanet.com/2020-01/27/c_1125504355.htm) reporter learned from the Chinese Center for Disease Control and Prevention on the 26th that the new coronavirus traceability study Phased progress was made in the first time. From the 585 environmental samples in the South China Seafood Market in Wuhan, 33 samples were detected containing novel coronavirus nucleic acids, and the virus was successfully isolated in positive environmental specimens, suggesting that the virus originated from the South China Seafood Market. wild animals. The reporter learned that on December 31, in accordance with the requirements of the Chinese Center for Disease Control, the virus disease selected an expert team to Wuhan to participate in epidemic prevention and control. On the morning of January 1, 2020, he went to the South China Seafood Market to collect 515 environmental samples from the case-related merchants and related blocks, and transported them to the viral disease office for testing. On January 12th, experts from the Viral Disease Institute collected 70 specimens from wild animal vendors in the South China Seafood Market again and transported them to the laboratory for testing. <br>
* The National Health and Health Commission released the new coronavirus-infected pneumonia situation [Seventh Announcement](http://www.nhc.gov.cn/xcs/yqtb/202001/3882fdcdbfdc4b4fa4e3a829b62d518e.shtml) as of January 26 24 At that time, a total of 2,744 confirmed cases were reported in 30 provinces (autonomous regions and municipalities) in the country, and Malaysia was newly diagnosed overseas. At the same time, the [Notice on Printing and Distributing New Coronavirus Infected Pneumonia Treatment Plan (Trial Version 4)](http://www.nhc.gov.cn/yzygj/s7653p/202001/4294563ed35b43209b31739bd0785e67.shtml). <br>
* Entrusted by General Secretary Xi Jinping, Premier Li Keqiang (Leader of the Central Leading Group for Response to Pneumonia in New Coronavirus Infections) went to Han to inspect and guide the prevention and control of the epidemic. See [Hubei Daily News](http://www.hubei.gov.cn/zwgk/hbyw/hbywqb/202001/t20200128_2015593.shtml) report on January 28. <br>
* The General Office of the State Council issued ["Notice on Extending the 2020 Spring Festival Holidays"](http://www.gov.cn/zhengce/content/2020-01/27/content_5472352.htm) and decided to extend the 2020 Spring Festival holidays to February 2 (the ninth day of the first lunar month, Sunday), and February 3 (Monday) to work normally. <br>

Azah said that President Trump and himself showed a transparent attitude toward the Chinese government in epidemic prevention and control The ongoing health cooperation is appreciated, and we welcome the WHO and other parties to work closely with China to fight the epidemic. That night [Wuhan Urban and Rural Construction Bureau](https://baijiahao.baidu.com/s?id=1657214500285625277) clarified that a construction unit was preparing to dig the site construction road to lay sewage pipes around 8:20 in the evening. The construction road is On the main road where construction materials and equipment enter and exit, the lifting of the on-site box house will be interrupted, which will seriously affect the construction of the Huoshen Mountain Project. The management personnel of another construction unit stepped forward to prevent the road excavation time There was a misunderstanding, which led to the push of the dispute, and was quickly dissuaded by the surrounding people to separate, and no one was injured. <br>

As a public health expert, I hope to talk to them and hope to learn something from them. Eight people are said to be the first-line doctors in the early stage of the epidemic. See [Picture Information](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/13#issue-557477266). <br>
* [CCTV News](https://weibo.com/2656274875/IrPHuzIcR) reported that the new coronavirus infection pneumonia, Shanghai Medical Treatment Expert Group Leader Zhang Wenhong said in an interview that he will be the first-line doctor of the infectious department on duty from New Year to now Change the post and change to the doctor of the Communist Party to work in the field. <br>

【International】 <br>
* "New England Medical Journal" published a paper ["New Coronavirus Infected Pneumonia in Wuhan, China, the initial transmission dynamics"](https://www.nejm.org/doi/pdf/10.1056/NEJMoa2001316), the corresponding author is Feng Zijian, deputy director of China CDC, Yang Bo, director of Hubei CDC, and Gao Fu, director of CDC are co-authors. Based on the analysis of 425 confirmed cases (including 15 medical staff) reported as of January 23, 2020, the paper concludes that the characteristics of human-to-human transmission have been established by the end of December. The article stated that medical personnel in Wuhan had been infected from January 1 to 11. The next day, [NEJM Medical Frontier WeChat Official Account](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/4MrNMiGWdvEDlyKyHviDiQ) reprinted the abstract, which was distributed on the domestic network. According to Eric Lushi, editor-in-chief of the New England Journal of Medicine, the paper took only 48 hours from submission to publication. <br>
