* Zeng Guang, the chief expert in epidemiology of the Chinese Center for Disease Control and Prevention, was interviewed by Hu Xijin, and a dialogue can be seen as a response. Zeng Guang said that Wuhan ’s slow action in the face of the epidemic was mainly a matter of scientific understanding, but it did not rule out some decision-making hesitation and whether he was confident in himself. Public health personnel's decision-making considers scientific issues and is a scientific perspective. However, government officials' consideration of issues is not simply a scientific perspective. This is only part of their decision-making basis. "He has to consider the political perspective, the issue of maintaining stability, he has to consider the issue of economy, he has to consider the happiness of the Chinese New Year, satisfaction and dissatisfaction. What we say is often only part of their decision." <Br >

Academician Gao Fu, one of the signed authors, boarded Weibo. <br>

【China】 <br>
* In the early morning, the National Health and Health Commission issued [Eleventh Announcement](http://www.nhc.gov.cn/xcs/yqfkdt/202001/a53e6df293cc4ff0b5a16ddf7b6b2b31.shtml), as of January 30, 24 provinces, 31 provinces (Autonomous regions, municipalities directly under the Central Government) and the Xinjiang Production and Construction Corps reported 1982 newly diagnosed cases, accumulatively reported 9692 confirmed cases (a cumulative reduction of confirmed cases in Sichuan Province), and a cumulative death case of 213 cases. <br>
* In the morning, [Chinese Center for Disease Control and Prevention](https://weibo.com/1618051664/IrZME2tAE) responded by publishing in the New England Journal entitled "New Coronavirus Infected Pneumonia in the Initial Transmission Dynamics of Wuhan, China" The paper is based on a retrospective analysis of 425 confirmed cases (including 15 medical staff) reported as of January 23, 2020, and all cases have been published to the public before the paper was written. The view that “the interpersonal transmission occurred in close contacts in December 2019” is based on the retrospective inferences made by the epidemiological investigation data of 425 cases. <br>
* At 9 o'clock, Xinhuanet's WeChat push article ["Quick and busy prevention and control, don't grab the paper!" 》](Https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/U1MRt76s0GLVDwj9Q3dlSg), expressing “a critical moment in the nation ’s ambition to fight the epidemic, a small number of scientific researchers must not distract their energy and affect the current fight against the epidemic Development of work ". There was no express party involved in the thesis event. <br>
* At 14:00, [Caixin.com](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/24#issue-557963108) interviewed Yang Gonghuan, the former deputy director of the Chinese Center for Disease Control and Prevention, on the thesis of the New England Journal of Medicine Yang said, "Whether the expert knows the truth does not report, or reports but fails to take timely measures. The two are very different. The key facts need to be clarified. 'If you only blame the experts, things will change.'" <br>
* [First Finance](https://weibo.com/1618051664/Is1VoEVyb) The reporter interviewed Gao Fu, a member of the high-level expert group of the National Health and Health Commission and director of the Chinese Center for Disease Control and Prevention. Gao Fu responded to the incident of the thesis, "This is a retrospective analysis! I do n’t know what the disease is in mid-December, and the etiology is unclear. They are all inferences from investigating more than 400 cases of epidemiology! The days of Onset are all speculations. This is not understood by everyone! Mix epidemiological investigation with clinical diagnosis. "He also said that retrospective investigation is one of the duties of CDC, to find the culprit, retrospective investigation, and guide future prevention and control. "Our prevention and control has not stopped, and everyone has not slept for a month." <br>
* At 14:00, [Hu Xijin](https://weibo.com/1989660417/Is1JOyy5R) commented on the thesis event, "disagreeing that some people attacked Gao Fu and others’ motives for publishing papers from an ethical perspective, accusing them of knowing the epidemic. In a very serious situation, the case was deliberately concealed from the country, and the case was published in a foreign journal and sold out to sell its reputation. " <br>
* At 17:00, Feng Zijian, one of the corresponding authors of the New England Journal of Medicine's thesis event and deputy director of the Chinese Center for Disease Control, accepted the [New Beijing News reporter interview](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/31 # issue-558086593) said that the above inference was made after obtaining the case data on January 23 and did not hide it. Viruses have been inferred for a long time, and there are reasons for conservative conclusions. He also said that "it is not particularly clear" whether CDC has received any suspected infection from medical staff. According to him, there are many levels of data reporting, including national, provincial, municipal, and district levels. "There is a process for data reporting, and I did not understand this process in detail." This also shows that the direct infectious disease reporting system has not been activated at this time. <br>
* "Intellectuals" WeChat public account released ["concealed" or "conservative"? A paper caused controversy in Wuhan epidemic](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/HWYGQ_SfvblAORygJwMs1w). <br>
* At 18 o'clock, the interface news Weibo published an article [Girls in Fan Circle Wuhan: We are "solving difficulties every day"](https://weibo.com/5182171545/Is3ds1b9a). <br>
* At 22:00, [People's Daily Weibo](https://weibo.com/2803301701/Is58Rg5zr) announced that the Shanghai Institute of Pharmacy and Wuhan Virus Research Institute jointly discovered that Shuanghuanglian can inhibit a new coronavirus. The study was led by Academician Jiang Hualiang. That night triggered a panic buying "Shuanghuanglian". <br>
* At 13:00 on the same day, Political Theories reprinted an excerpt from the old article "Social Psychological Analysis of the Spreading Distortion on the Rumor of" SARS "" [周晓虹:Distortion of Spreading: A Social Psychological Analysis of the Rumor on "Atypical Pneumonia"](https : //mp.weixin.qq.com/s/sXrlF9lMbeDmNAfcTl86NQ). <br>

There are more than 30 boxes of materials. The next day he settled in the East Campus of Wuhan University People's Hospital. Patients. ["Changjiang Daily"](https://weibo.com/1898268644/IsxFSy8kf) reports. <br>

February 11 [Guangzhou Municipal Commission for Discipline Inspection and Supervision](http://www.gzjjjc.gov.cn/gzsjw/tbgz/202002/50495f7044ad41529348712a33dc1175.shtml) notified from January 28 to February 6 Chief physician Chen Jiandong (non-Party member, career establishment cadre) and social personnel Huang Moumou reselling masks for profit. Huang Moumou is responsible for providing masks and supplying the goods, and Chen Jiandong is responsible for pushing sales. The Discipline Inspection and Supervision Group of the Municipal Commission of Discipline Inspection and Supervision Commission in the Municipal Health and Health Commission made a punishment for Chen Jiandong to reduce the level of technical posts and collected his illegal income. <br>

It also mentioned that the United States has been notified of the epidemic information and prevention and control measures 30 times since January 3. Together with the control of the port control zone implemented on the 30th of last month, the number of ports temporarily suspended from providing passenger clearance services will be increased to ten. <br>

## February 4, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
* [Website of Hubei Provincial Commission for Discipline Inspection](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/rYrRiy6mjk8Vxzj1Gg7sWQ) notified that three leaders of the Hubei Provincial Red Cross Society were held accountable. CCTV News WeChat official account is reproduced. <br>
* The Publicity Working Group of Wuhan New Pneumonia Prevention and Control Headquarters issued a statement [Notice](http://www.wuhan.gov.cn/hbgovinfo/zwgk_8265/tzgg/202002/t20200204_304404.html). The work found that many citizens recently Distribute information about yourself or relatives and friends for help through various Internet platforms, reflecting problems such as difficult detection and treatment. The propaganda working group verified the contact information provided in the relevant districts and information. As of February 3, 135 requests for help received positive responses from relevant districts and departments, and patients have been properly placed. <br>
* [Governor of Chang'an Street](https://www.takefoto.cn/viewnews-2034585.html): Wuhan is stepping up the construction of three "square cabin hospitals" in Jianghan District, Wuchang District and Dongxihu District, which are located in Wuhan International Convention and Exhibition Center, Hongshan Stadium, Wuhan living room. The latest news is that after a busy night, at 8:58 am on the 4th, Wuhan Hongshan Gymnasium has transformed into a 800-bed "square cabin hospital", waiting for the arrival of mild patients with new coronavirus pneumonia. <br>
* [Surging News: A volunteer in Wuhan died after infection, and was obliged to take care of medical staff to work](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/yigRCNdk8_aWy7w3UJGE9g) reported on the Wuhan volunteer team, 54-year-old He Hui, He died at the Sino-French New Town district of Tongji Hospital at 4 pm yesterday. <br>
* [Secondary Six Seven Seven Eight Weibo](https://weibo.com/2158017273/IsFhm8uKM) released: I set up an 8-episode video of "My Vulcan Mountain Construction Diary" in a hospital in an epidemic area. <br>

【China】 <br>
* At 2 o'clock, [issued by the Hangzhou Municipal People's Government](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/xUxTWicvDbdstE8wT0W8fw) notice on the implementation of the ten measures of "prevention and control of epidemic situation, everyone is responsible". All villages, communities and units in the city implement closed-end management, and the temperature of people entering and exiting shall be measured at all times, and valid certificates shall be issued. <br>
* The National Health and Construction Commission Li Lanjuan team announced the results of in vitro cell experiments for the treatment of new coronavirus infections. <br>
* ["Jinjiang Poison King Incident"](https://archive.li/Wc9Ns) fermented online. The family of Zhang Fang, Jiapai Village, Yinglin Town, Jinjiang City, Fujian knew that they were from Wuhan, but they lied to the villagers that they were from the Philippines. They did not carry out house isolation in accordance with the regulations. They also participated in banquets and went out frequently. On February 1, Zhang Fang was diagnosed with New Coronary Pneumonia. He had conducted home medical observations on 91 people, and conducted medical follow-up and control of 3557 general contacts. <br>
* [Hong Kong Wireless News](https://weibo.com/2615417307/IsD6eAXWN) news, the Macao SAR Chief Executive He Yicheng said that in order to prevent the spread of the epidemic, Macau decided to suspend the gaming industry and related entertainment industry for half a month. <br>
* In the evening, the Nanjing New Coronavirus Infected Pneumonia Joint Prevention and Control Command Headquarters issued [Announcement](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/_OAx06R2M9OVTKNIPCVdnw) to fully implement closed-end management of the community. On the same day [Harbin](https://weibo.com/2803301701/IsFJ20EXU), the community and villages where confirmed cases and suspected cases have occurred should be listed to prevent people and vehicles from entering and exiting. <br>
* Nanjing University [Sun Jiang: I ca n’t forgive even if I start again tomorrow](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/dXl87F2V3skO7J9PYVICsw) <br>
* Wu Xiaohua released ["Everything I Know and You Should Know"](https://card.weibo.com/article/m/show/id/2309634468392248606935), continue to question the original virus of 2019-nCoV, which is kept in Wuhan Shi Zhengli's virus bank in the Virus Research Institute proposed that she published a paper in the electronic journal of natural medicine in 2015, saying that as long as the ACE2 receptor switch in the S protein of the bat is adjusted, the virus can be transmitted immediately. To humans. For the rest, please refer to [Shi Zhengli VS Wu Xiaohua Incident Related Collation](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/70#issue-560103415). <br>
* VOA released in Chinese [Hong Kong ’s first 39-year-old man died after diagnosis of Wuhan pneumonia], Hong Kong Health Protection Center released at 4 o’clock, a 39-year-old man with Wuhan pneumonia died, this is the first local death case in Hong Kong After the Philippines, the second death case outside China. <br>
* [Stand News](https://www.thestandnews.com/society/%E6%9C%AA%E6%9C%89%E7%89%87-%E9%86%AB%E8%AD%B7% E7% BD% B7% E5% B7% A5% E5% 8D% 87% E7% B4% 9A-% E5% 8D% 83% E4% BA% BA% E9% 81% 9E% E4% BF% A1% E8 % AB% 8B% E9% A1% 98% E6% B1% 82% E5% B0% 81% E9% 97% 9C-% E9% AA% A8% E7% A7% 91% E9% 86% AB% E7% 94% 9F-% E8% 80% 8C% E5% AE% B6% E6% 83% 85% E6% B3% 81% E6% 85% 98% E9% 81% 8E% E6% B2% 99% E5% A3 % AB): Medical care strikes escalated. Thousands of people sent letters petitioning for customs clearance. The negotiation between the "HA Staff Front" and the HA broke down. More than 7,000 people participated in the second stage strike action, accounting for nearly 10% of all HA staff. Some emergency services of public hospitals are affected.

## February 5, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
* Released by Caixin.com ["Mainly in the elderly in patients with fever in multiple gates of Baibuting Community in Wuhan"](http://m.china.caixin.com/m/2020-02-05/101511619.html) . <br>
* The first batch of patients was admitted to Wuhan Fangcai Hospital. [Xinhua News Agency](https://m.weibo.cn/status/4469012366538691) The reporter photographed a patient lying on a hospital bed and was reading Fushan's "The Origin of Political Order". <br>
* Hubei Honghu City Market Supervision and Administration Bureau has filed an investigation into Honghu Huakang Large Pharmacy for allegedly inflating the price of masks. After investigation, Honghu Huakang Pharmacy sold 38,000 disposable masks at a purchase price of 0.6 yuan / piece and a sales price of 1 yuan / piece. The difference between the purchase and sales was higher than the "Provincial Market Supervision Bureau on the prevention of pneumonia caused by new coronavirus infections". The 15% standard stipulated in the Guiding Opinions on the Determination and Handling of Price Illegal Acts during the Control Period (Eshijian Competition [2020] No. 3) is suspected of driving up prices. At present, the Honghu City Market Supervision Administration has concluded the investigation of the case, confiscating the illegal income of 14,210 yuan and a fine of 42,630 yuan. See [Report] on February 12 (https://weibo.com/1638782947/ItQDky4D4). <br>
* At 21:00, Hubei Province [New Coronavirus Infection Pneumonia Prevention and Control Command](http://www.hubei.gov.cn/zhuanti/2020/gzxxgzbd/zxtb/202002/t20200205_2019807.shtml) issued an order: the province New coronavirus-infected pneumonia designated hospitals and various medical institutions at all levels will do their best to treat the suspected and confirmed cases found. If it cannot be admitted, register in accordance with relevant regulations, and promptly notify the county (city, district) epidemic prevention and control headquarters or the jurisdictional transshipment team. The county (city, district) epidemic prevention and control headquarters or the jurisdictional transshipment team will arrange vehicles to be transferred to a centralized location. Quarantine points to ensure that suspected and confirmed cases are "receiving as much as possible, treating as soon as possible", and ensuring that no one is spared. Those who violate this article shall be held accountable in strict accordance with the relevant provisions of the Law on the Prevention and Control of Infectious Diseases. <br>

【China】 <br>
* In the afternoon, the National Health and Health Commission issued ["Diagnosis and Treatment Plan for New Coronavirus Infected Pneumonia (Trial Version 5)"](http://www.nhc.gov.cn/yzygj/s7652m/202002/e84bd30142ab4d8982326326e4db22ea.shtml) . The diagnosis and treatment plan adds a "clinical diagnosis case" in addition to "suspected cases" and "confirmed cases", and uses "suspected cases with pneumonia imaging features" as its diagnostic criteria (only within Hubei Province), which also This means that the CT imaging results have become the basis for "clinical diagnosis cases". Zhang Xiaochun, deputy director of the imaging department of Wuhan University's Central South Hospital, has previously implemented the appeal of the circle of friends. <br>
* The student dormitories in the Mainland of Hong Kong Baptist University are used as new corona virus isolation areas. See [Hong Kong Baptist University Mainland student Weibo_PoJackma](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/77#issue-560862330) <br>
* [CCTV News](https://weibo.com/2656274875/IsO5RBy2p) reported that Zhang Moumou, a villager in Jiapai Village, Yinglin Town, Jinjiang, Fujian Province, returned from Wuhan and concealed the itinerary to participate in local folk events and banquet dinners. On February 1, Zhang Moumou was diagnosed. Local people have been conducting home-based medical observation on 91 people, and 3557 general contacts have been followed up and controlled throughout the medical process. <br>
* In the evening, the Liaoning Provincial People's Government issued ["Notice on Printing and Distributing 30 Articles of Strict Investigation and Strict Control Measures for Urban and Rural Communities (Villages)" (http://www.ln.gov.cn/zfxx/jrln/wzxx2018/ 202002 / t20200205_3734347.html), requiring closed management of villages and residential communities. <br>
* [GQ report: Rice Circle Rescue 2020](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/Wj0P1aT-1oHRbVij_Icbgg) <br>
* [National Internet Information Office](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/YhjV75NwJZO4CyPdepArQw) guides relevant local Internet Information Offices to investigate and deal with illegal website platforms and accounts in accordance with law. We will promptly deal with issues such as illegal self-acquisition and dissemination of false information on online accounts such as "Netease Finance", "Sina Weitian", "Gu Yu Lab", and "Best Meow in History". <br>
* [BBC 中文](/ amp / s / www.bbc.com / zhongwen / simp / amp / chinese-news-51386084): 16:30, Hong Kong Chief Executive Zheng Yuee held a press conference and announced that he would quote "Prevention and Control" The power of Chapter 599 of the Disease Regulations to enact subsidiary legislation will begin on February 8th, requiring all people who enter the mainland of China, regardless of nationality, to undergo mandatory quarantine for 14 days, during which they must not leave the country. <br>
* Sanlian Life Weekly's Weibo was banned for a week, and the information transfer affiliate Zhongdu was released. <br>

【International】 <br>
* In the morning, the Japanese Ministry of Health, Labor and Welfare announced that it had confirmed that a new coronavirus pneumonia collective infection (10 persons) was currently anchored in the large cruise ship "Diamond Princess" carrying more than 3,700 passengers off the coast of Yokohama Port. Japan ’s Minister of Health, Labour and Welfare Kato Shinto said at a press conference on February 5 that “we require passengers to stay on the ship for a maximum of 14 days and will do their best to respond.” The cruise ship is from January 20 to February 4. , Is in the multi-point docking voyage of "16 days of Southeast Asia in early spring". The ship "Diamond Princess" left Hong Kong from Yokohama on January 20 and arrived in Hong Kong on January 25 after docking in Kagoshima, Japan. Subsequently, the ship sailed to Vietnam, Taiwan and other places, docked in Okinawa, Japan on February 1, and returned to Yokohama on February 3. See [Caixin.com A cruise ship found more than 3,700 people in Yokohama, Japan, who were quarantined at sea for 14 days](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/byhpOMxt4NX9n00bGZZYxg). <br>
* [Stand News: American Airlines and United Airlines suspend flights to and from Hong Kong after China to Hong Kong](https://www.thestandnews.com/international/%E4%B8%AD%E5%9C%8B%E4%B9%8B % E5% BE% 8C% E5% 88% B0% E9% A6% 99% E6% B8% AF-% E7% BE% 8E% E5% 9C% 8B% E8% 88% AA% E7% A9% BA- % E8% 81% AF% E5% 90% 88% E8% 88% AA% E7% A9% BA% E6% 9A% AB% E5% 81% 9C% E5% BE% 80% E8% BF% 94% E9 % A6% 99% E6% B8% AF% E8% 88% AA% E7% 8F% AD /), United Airlines announced that it will stop all flights to and from Hong Kong from Saturday until the 20th of this month. The grounding arrangements mean that no US civil aircraft will travel to or from Hong Kong after this week. <br>

Strengthen grid management, or leave one household and one person. <br>

Pay tribute to fight against the epidemic and express sincere condolences to his family. <br>

Concentrated isolation of suspected patients is currently an urgent task. <br>

The disease control department believes that they underreported underreported cases at the end of December and early January. The doctor objected: "The health and health committee requires three conditions to report at the same time. It did not meet the three conditions at that time." ## 2020 February 8 yen festival
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>

* On the same day, Chen Yixin will be the deputy leader of the Central Steering Group. <br>
* According to CCTV reports, the first batch of medical team members of the Raytheon Mountain Hospital in Wuhan has been stationed and will accept the first batch of patients. At this point, the two hospitals of Vulcan Mountain and Thunder Mountain have all been delivered. <br>
* At 13:00, [Central Discipline Inspection Commission National Supervision Commission website](http://www.ccdi.gov.cn/toutiao/202002/t20200208_211082.html) News: The National Supervision Commission investigation team arrived in Wuhan. <br>
* At 19:50, the official Weibo of Wuhan Vulcan Hill Hospital went online and claimed to be "Little Fire". On February 10, the Weibo was deactivated.

【China】 <br>
* The State Council Joint Defense and Joint Control Mechanism held a [press conference](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/W3hZF7YnHf2wyNqw-VAYKw), and a spokesperson for the National Health and Welfare Commission issued a notice on the temporary naming of pneumonia infected by the new crown virus : Pneumonia infected with new coronavirus is collectively referred to as "new coronavirus pneumonia", referred to as "new coronavirus pneumonia", English name "Novel coronavirus pneumonia", referred to as "NCP". <br>
* On the same day, the National Health Construction Commission issued [Notice on Printing and Distributing New Coronavirus Pneumonia Diagnosis and Treatment Program (Trial Version 5 Revision)](http://www.nhc.gov.cn/yzygj/s7653p/202002/d4b895337e19445f8d728fcaf1e3e13a.shtml) . <br>
* [Shanghai Epidemic Prevention and Control Work Press Conference](https://weibo.com/2656274875/ItfKK3qJv) Introduction: Health and epidemic prevention experts emphasized that the current routes of transmission of new coronary pneumonia are mainly direct transmission, aerosol transmission and contact transmission. Aerosol transmission means that droplets are mixed in the air to form an aerosol, which causes infection after inhalation. <br>
* The Ministry of Finance and the State Administration of Taxation: The longest carry-over period for the losses of enterprises in difficult industries affected by the epidemic in 2020 will be extended from 5 to 8 years. <br>
* [Hong Kong Special Administrative Region Government Press Release](https://www.info.gov.hk/gia/general/202002/07/P2020020700737.htm) from the early morning of February 8, the Department of Health Persons from Hong Kong (including Hong Kong residents, mainland residents and visitors from other regions) issue quarantine orders. The persons concerned must be subject to quarantine at home or other residence for 14 days. Quarantine persons must stay in their homes or related residences at all times and wear masks, and are prohibited from leaving Hong Kong. Unauthorized leaving the residence will constitute a criminal offence. Once convicted, he can be imprisoned for six months and fined 25,000 yuan. Government officials will make sure that the person undergoing compulsory quarantine stays in the residence through unannounced inspections and calling the person. <br>

【International】 <br>
* Lianhe Zaobao: World Health Organization Director General Tan Desai warned on Friday that just as the world was struggling to deal with the new crown, medical protective clothing, masks, gloves and other protective products faced a chronic shortage. <br>
* [China News Service](https://m.chinanews.com/wap/detail/zw/gj/2020/02-08/9083357.shtml) Tokyo, February 8th (Reporter Lu Shaowei) is anchored in Yokohama, Japan On the 8th, the cruise ship "Diamond Princess", which underwent large-scale quarantine offshore, received news that three of the six newly identified results confirmed the infection and had been taken to the hospital urgently. A total of 89 cases were diagnosed in Japan. <br>

## February 9, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
* Hubei Province held the 19th epidemic prevention and control work press conference. Academician of the Chinese Academy of Engineering, expert of Hubei Province New Coronary Pneumonia Epidemic Prevention and Control Research Group, and Professor Huanchun Zhang of Huazhong Agricultural University said that "the new coronavirus belongs to SARS coronavirus", CCTV News Weibo reported at 21:00. Later, Zhang Huanchun changed his vocabulary to "spoken language". The correlation between the two was not the same. CCTV News Weibo deleted related blog posts. In the same night, Zhong Nanshan was interviewed by the First Business Finance and said that the two are parallel and different in kind. Xu Wenbo, director of the Chinese Center for Disease Control and Prevention, said in a telephone interview with [First Financial](https://news.sina.cn/gn/2020-02-09/detail-iimxyqvz1559555.d.html) that the new coronavirus It is a new virus, not a SARS virus. <br>
* Wuhan Software Engineering Vocational College received a notice from the Wuhan City Office of Prevention and Control on the 7th, and was urgently requisitioned as a new coronary pneumonia isolation point. When school staff returned to school to clean up, they randomly discarded students ’personal belongings, which caused heated discussions on the Internet. At 23:00, [Wubo Software Engineering College Youth League Weibo](https://weibo.com/2619766381/ItsVqprci) issued a letter of apology. <br>
* It is reported that the luggage of the Jiangsu Medical Team was lost, and the materials of the Hubei Medical Team were detained. Afterwards, officials from the Jiangsu Communist Youth League and other officials dispelled rumors. <br>
* On the same day, Wuhan citizen Fang Bin, who published [Wuhan Epidemic Video](https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCRItarzSwqakT-EZkSvuy3A/videos) on the Internet, lost contact with the outside world. See [They Documented the Coronavirus Crisis in Wuhan. Then They Vanished](https://www.nytimes.com/2020/02/14/business/wuhan-coronavirus-journalists.html). <br>

【China】 <br>
* The quarantine of the "World Dream" cruise ship with confirmed patients with new coronary pneumonia has been completed, and the test results of all the crew's new coronaviruses are negative, and they are about to disembark. The cruise ship anchored at Kai Tak Cruise Terminal in Hong Kong for five days. <br>
* The "Clinical Characteristics of New Coronavirus Infections in China in 2019" led by Zhong Nanshan was published on the preprint website [medRxiv](https://www.medrxiv.org/content/10.1101/2020.02.06.20020974v1). Zhong Nanshan et al. Conducted a retrospective study of the clinical characteristics of 1099 patients (as of January 29) who had been diagnosed with new coronary pneumonia. The study found that the median incubation period of new coronary pneumonia is 3.0 days, up to 24 days. Domestic [surging news](https://www.thepaper.cn/newsDetail_forward_5895180) reported on the 10th. <br>
* [Hong Kong Department of Health Centre for Health Protection](https://www.info.gov.hk/gia/general/202002/09/P2020020900701.htm) The Centre for Health Protection of the Department of Health announced that as of today (February 9) evening At 8 o'clock, the center is investigating 10 newly diagnosed cases of new coronavirus infections, including a 24-year-old man who has attended the family's fireside party, and 8 relatives who attended the party together. So far, there have been 36 confirmed cases in Hong Kong. <br>

【International】 <br>
* [Weibo of the US Embassy in China](https://weibo.com/1743951792/ItgBw2Ikt): [US State Department](https://translations.state.gov/2020/02/07/the-united-states -announces-assistance-to-combat-the-novel-coronavirus /) assist in the delivery of medical supplies of nearly 17.8 metric tons. These supplies include important items such as masks, protective clothing, gauze, and respirators. <br>
* The cruise ship "Diamond Princess" docked in Yokohama, Japan confirmed another 6 patients with new coronary pneumonia. A total of 70 cases have been diagnosed on this cruise. This is the fifth day that passengers and crew on the cruise ship were quarantined, and all patients were sent to the hospital for treatment after diagnosis. <br>
* [UK Guardian](https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/feb/09/sars-whistleblower-doctor-under-house-arrest-in-china-family-confirms-jiang-yangyong ): In 2003, Jiang Yanyong, a Chinese doctor known internationally for exposing the Chinese government to cover up the SARS epidemic, is still under house arrest. Now 88 years old. Dr. Jiang Yanyong wrote to the highest leadership of the Chinese government in 2019, requesting him to re-evaluate the patriotism movement in support of democracy on June 4th, and the act of writing directly led him to be forced to disconnect from the outside world, according to a close friend of his. From the beginning of the month, Dr. Jiang was placed under house arrest. Today, Dr. Jiang Yanyong, 88, is in great physical and mental health. Dr. Jiang, who suffered from pneumonia, was treated at 301 Hospital. During this period, he was closely monitored and prevented from visiting by anyone. It is reported that the doctor ’s brain is affected by the drugs received and the memory Seriously lost. <br>
* [Caixin.com](https://m.international.caixin.com/m/2020-02-09/101513333.html) reported that in the recent days, through the expressions of North Korean official media, it can be learned that in early February Within a few days, North Korea ’s epidemic prevention measures and command system have undergone a wave of escalation—from focusing on epidemic prevention to border prevention and control and screening personnel with a history of exit, expanding to all parts of North Korea and tracking Screen the key prevention and control objects that have entered the country, and strengthen publicity. North Korea has not yet notified the World Health Organization of any confirmed cases. <br>

## February 10, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
* On February 10, [Hubei Provincial Party Committee Standing Committee](https://wap.peopleapp.com/article/5137898/5035821) decided to remove Zhang Jin ’s position as party secretary of the Provincial Health and Health Committee; Liu Yingzi ’s The post of director of the Provincial Health Commission; the above two posts are concurrently served by the newly appointed Comrade Wang Hesheng of the Provincial Standing Committee. <br>
* [Hubei Provincial Department of Housing and Urban-Rural Development](http://zjt.hubei.gov.cn/fbjd/xxgkml/zcwj/202002/t20200210_2023457.shtml) released the "About the Issuance of New Coronavirus Pneumonia in Residential Areas and Office Buildings in Hubei Province" Notice of "Guide to Prevention and Control Work". The notice pointed out that the residential area should be closed. In principle, only one entrance is reserved. Personnel must measure and register their body temperature. It is strictly forbidden for visitors who have a temperature of more than 37.3 ° C to enter and exit; temporarily close the clubhouse, library, activity room and other personnel gathering places in the community , Restrict the entry of non-resident personnel and vehicles into residential communities (including couriers, takeaways, etc.) <br>
* In the afternoon, Liang Mou, a 70-year-old patient with suspected new coronary pneumonia, jumped off the building in the Jiangwan New Town Community, Qiaokou District, Wuhan City. According to the [Economic Observation Network](https://news.sina.com.cn/s/2020-02-12/doc-iimxxstf0845452.shtml) interview with Liang ’s son Liang Xin, the parents are suspected of being infected with new coronary pneumonia. He did not live with his parents, was isolated in his home in Hanyang District, and took care of two children. When his father jumped the stairs, only his mother was present. He only left a message to his mother, "I don't want to cause you any trouble," and he turned the railing down with his hand. <br>
* In the evening, Hubei Province held a [New Coronary Pneumonia Epidemic Prevention and Control Press Conference](https://weibo.com/1784473157/ItAYkdT3p), introduced by Zhang Dingyu, deputy secretary and dean of the Party Committee of Jinyintan Hospital in Wuhan City, which is actually a kind of Limited disease. "The cure rate in our hospital is still very high. More than 1,500 patients with new coronary pneumonia have been admitted to our hospital at present. The vast majority of patients, including severe and critically ill patients, have undergone various oxygen treatments, symptomatic treatments and After immunomodulatory treatment, they can all be discharged smoothly, and the citizens do not have to panic too much. "<br>
* At about 22 o'clock, at the door of a hospital in Wuhan, Hubei, a girl followed the funeral car and cried out "Mom". The photographer introduced that the girl's mother was a suspected patient of the new coronavirus pneumonia and was sent to the Hubei Provincial Hospital of Integrated Traditional Chinese and Western Medicine. She died after the rescue failed. Because of the epidemic, the mother could only be taken away and directly cremated. As of February 9, a total of investigations have been conducted. In 3371 communities and villages, 4.21 million households and 10.59 million were surveyed by households. The proportion of household surveys reached 98.6%, and the proportion of population surveys reached 99%. Tomorrow, all suspected patient tests will be cleared. 【International】 <br>
* [International Virus Taxonomy Committee](https://talk.ictvonline.org/) (International Committee on Taxonomy of Viruses, (ICTV)) recently announced that the virus with the temporary name of 2019-nCoV (2019 new coronavirus) was Officially named SARS-CoV-2 (severe acute respiratory syndrome coronavirus type 2). Previously, [World Health Organization](https://twitter.com/WHO/status/1227248333871173632) had named the disease caused by the virus as COVID-19, and the Chinese Health and Health Commission had previously named the disease caused by the virus as " New Coronavirus Pneumonia (NCP) ". <br>

The data shows that according to the date of onset, before December 31, 2019 There were 104 infected people, and 15 of them died. Before January 10, 113 counties in 20 provinces had been distributed. The paper also explained the concept of "date of onset". For the epidemiological curve, the date of onset was defined as the date when the case self-reported the onset of fever or cough in the epidemiological investigation. <br>

## February 14, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
* Wuhan City's New Coronary Pneumonia Epidemic Prevention and Control Command issued [Notice](https://weibo.com/2759348142/Iue90cPDD), which clarified the main measures for the closed management of residential communities. This is also the detailed and clear regulations made by the prevention and control command on the announcement on February 10 in the form of formal notice. The notice requires that when closed management is carried out on residential quarters, only one entrance and exit is reserved for each quarter. Old quarters and open-plan residential areas are hard-segregated by siege. Arrange personnel at the entrance and exit 24 hours on duty, register for temperature measurement, review and release. Except for medical staff, epidemic prevention, and operation guarantee, other residents are not allowed to go out. <br>
* At 4:51, the director of Hubei Film Studio's "Xianyinxiang" External Liaison Department [Chang Fan](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/102#issue-565880372) in Huangbei, Wuhan The People's Hospital passed away at the age of 55. 【China】 <br>
* In the afternoon, the State Council Office held a press conference on the latest progress in epidemic prevention and control, especially the measures for caring for medical personnel. Zeng Yixin, deputy director of the National Health and Health Commission, said at the press conference that in accordance with the relevant regulations of the epidemic situation, only suspected cases of new coronary pneumonia and external Confirmed cases. Asymptomatic infections are not cases and need not be announced. If an asymptomatic infected person develops symptoms during concentrated isolation, we can use it as a confirmed case report at this time and publish it externally. Asymptomatic infection refers to those who have no clinical symptoms, but who have a positive detection of new coronavirus in the respiratory tract and other specimens. For details, see February 26 [Caixin · Interpretation:Controversial New Crown Asymptomatic Infected Persons: Why not be included in the diagnosis statistics](http://china.caixin.com/2020-02-26/101520417.html)<br >

* [CCTV News](https://wap.peopleapp.com/article/5156381/5055261): Recently, under the guidance of Academician Zhong Nanshan, the laboratory has jointly developed a number of research institutes to develop the latest rapid detection of new coronavirus IgM antibodies The kit has been completed in the laboratory and clinical preliminary evaluation. According to reports, only one drop of blood can be used to visually observe the test result within 15 minutes, and the patient's plasma can still detect a positive band after being diluted 500 to 1000 times. <br>
* [China Daily](https://weibo.com/2127460165/IukTGksbG): learned from the Ministry of Transport, with the consent of the State Council, from 0:00 on February 17 to the end of the epidemic prevention and control work, the national toll roads will be free of vehicles toll. An 83-year-old American woman who flew from Cambodia to Malaysia was diagnosed with a positive test for her new coronavirus. The cruise liner was moored at Sihanoukville in southwest Cambodia on the 13th and carried 1,455 passengers and 802 crew members. According to reports, the cruise ship was refused docking by Japan, Taiwan, Guam, the Philippines and Thailand, and drifted on the sea for two weeks. <br>

【China】 <br>
* The National Health and Safety Commission issued ["New Coronavirus Pneumonia Diagnosis and Treatment Program (Trial Version 6)"](http://www.nhc.gov.cn/yzygj/s7652m/202002/54e1ad5c2aac45c19eb541799bf637e9.shtml): Diagnostic criteria canceled Hubei The difference between provinces and provinces other than Hubei Province. They are uniformly divided into two categories: "suspected cases" and "confirmed cases". Confirmed cases require a positive result of the etiological evidence (real-time fluorescent RT-PCR detection of new coronavirus nucleic acid positive; or viral gene sequencing, highly homologous to known new coronavirus) The category of clinical diagnosis cases unique to Hubei Province was cancelled. In the trial drugs, two drugs "chloroquine phosphate" and "Abidor" were added. <br>

The following day the Ezhou government website released ["Notice on the Survey of Netizens 'Exposure of WeChat Users'" Advancing with Stone "Related Issues"](http://www.ezhou.gov.cn/zt/zdzt/fzyqmy/qwtb/202002 /t20200222_326144.html), pointed out that the WeChat user "advance with the stone" saw that the cherry tomatoes in the video of the Phoenix Police Station of the Shebei District Public Security Bureau were similar to the small tomatoes he bought, and he wanted to show off in the group. There are no public officials. The public security organs have already admonished them. <br>
* [Hubei Daily](https://weibo.com/2827102952/IvdvwilH3) The reporter learned from the Hubei Provincial Prison Administration that there are 271 confirmed cases of new coronary pneumonia in the provincial prison system, including 230 cases diagnosed in Wuhan Women ’s Prison and Shayang in Hubei Province 41 cases were diagnosed in Hanjin Prison, all of which were imported cases. At present, there are no deaths of prisoners in custody infected with new coronary pneumonia. The Wuhan Women's Prison in Hubei Province was removed from the post due to poor prevention and control. <br>
* [Xinhua Viewpoint](https://weibo.com/1699432410/IveHx2hTv): At the Hubei epidemic prevention and control press conference, the deputy director of the Hubei Provincial Health and Health Commission Tu Yuanchao said that these days the new crown pneumonia released by Hubei Province, especially Wuhan City The adjustment of data has aroused great concern of the society. In this regard, the Secretary of the Provincial Party Committee should pay great attention to Comrade Yong Yong, and clearly request that the reduction of confirmed cases should not be allowed, and all reductions must be added back, and the relevant responsible persons should investigate the facts and be seriously accountable. <br>
* [Hubei Health and Health Commission](http://wjw.hubei.gov.cn/fbjd/dtyw/202002/t20200221_2144867.shtml) Statement: On February 19, some municipalities and prefectures reported clinical diagnosis cases according to the first The sixth edition of the diagnosis and treatment plan was revised to reduce some of the confirmed cases. This wrong practice was discovered and stopped in time on February 20. The number of cases reduced on February 19 is now added back to the confirmed cases, and the number of new cases added on that day is revised. From 0-24 February 19th, the number of newly confirmed cases in the province was revised from 349 to 775, and the cumulative number of confirmed cases was revised from 62,031 to 62,457. At the same time, the cumulative number of confirmed cases in the province as of 24:00 on February 20 was revised from 62,662 to 63,088. <br>

* At 11 o'clock, Wuhan New Coronary Pneumonia Epidemic Prevention and Control Headquarters issued ["Notice on Strengthening Management of Vehicles and Personnel Entering and Exiting Wuhan" (No. 17)](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline / issues / 123 # issue-569688999), foreign personnel stranded in Wuhan and those who must leave the city due to epidemic protection reasons can leave the city. Persons leaving the city must not be quarantined and have no symptoms of fever or dry cough. Persons leaving the city must insist on going out of the city at the wrong peak, and submit to the Wuhan Municipal Epidemic Prevention Headquarters for examination and approval as required. The personnel going out of the city will be monitored for 14 days after arriving at the destination. <br>

## February 28, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
* At about 9:30 in the morning, 22 people from a group of 14 villagers in Xiangyao Village, Huangmei Town, Hubei Province, accidentally consumed chlorine dioxide environmental disinfection tablets and were rushed to the County People's Hospital for treatment. On the evening of February 29, a telegram about the matter suspected of being sent by the Huanggang City People's Government to the counties circulated online. The Propaganda Department of Huangmei County Party Committee confirmed to [Interface News](https://www.jiemian.com/article/4049983.html) that there was indeed a poisoning incident of accidental consumption of "disinfection tablets". On the afternoon of March 1, the Huangmei County People's Government website issued a circular to confirm. After investigation, on February 25, when Huangmei Town distributed protective materials to various village communities, they all explained the purpose and usage of effervescent tablets. Each effervescent tablet was mixed with 2 kg of water for spray disinfection in the residents' homes. Arrange to the village of Yaoyao village women director, accountant Luo Xiaohong and grid member Zhai Jinxia responsible for the distribution of materials to the groups. At 15:00 on the 27th, Luo Xiaohong called a group leader Jiang Jianjun to collect a set of protective materials from the village committee and distributed them to the villagers. However, the phone did not inform Jiang Jianjun of the purpose and use of effervescent tablets. <br>

* In the morning, Li Moumin of the third day of Dengzhou, Henan, swallowed a lot of her mother ’s medication for mental illness because she could n’t afford to buy a mobile phone and could n’t follow the school online class on time. It is understood that her father, Li Handang, has a disability in his left leg and can only make a living by repairing shoes on the street. The mother suffers from mental illness and has no ability to work. Her monthly medical expenses cost hundreds of dollars. Since the three children in the family are going to school and the daily expenses are not small, the village has designated their family as a poor household with a registered card. March 2 [Dengzhou People's Government](http://www.dengzhou.gov.cn/portal/zfxxgk/zfxxgkml/szfxxgkml/gsgg/webinfo/2020/03/1572755168108131.htm) released the announcement, the first time Arrange the hospital for full treatment. At present, Li is not in danger of life and his condition is stable. At the same time, an investigation team has been established to conduct an in-depth investigation into the cause of taking Li's medication. The investigation will be announced in time. <br>
* [Taiwan Ministry of Health and Welfare Department of Disease Control](https://www.cdc.gov.tw/Bulletin/Detail/mbmNaswS86akZ2X7Vt_-Aw?typeid=9): Taiwan Epidemic Epidemic Command Center announced on the 29th, the island has added 5 4 cases of new coronary pneumonia were diagnosed, 4 of which were contacts in a hospital in northern Taiwan before the diagnosis of the 34th case announced yesterday (28th). They were 1 cleaning staff (case 35) and 3 nursing staff (case 36). To 38). Case 35 had contacted Case 34 while working in the emergency department of the hospital. The remaining three persons were nurses who were admitted to the ward before the diagnosis of Case 34. Four persons successively developed symptoms such as cough, runny nose, and fever on February 18-25. After the diagnosis was confirmed, it was listed as the contact person's inspection. It was confirmed today as a group incident. <br>

Patients wear masks throughout. At 7 a.m. on February 29, the patient developed cough and fever. At 10 o'clock, his family drove to the 8th Affiliated Hospital of Sun Yat-sen University for a hot clinic. At 21 o'clock, pharyngeal swabs were screened positive for new coronavirus nucleic acid. At 23 o'clock, the patient was transferred to the Third People's Hospital of Shenzhen City for isolation treatment. His mother, the sister of Ayatollah ShobeiriZanjani, a senior Iranian cleric, also died of new pneumonia. <br>

The Jordanian patient returned to Jordan from Italy two weeks ago and was immediately quarantined when he arrived in Jordan. <br>

## March 3, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
* At noon, [Wuhan Central Hospital](https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/qb-yEgwoRLKUQpCGHO_pNA) ophthalmologist Mei Zhongming passed away due to a new coronary pneumonia infection. He and Li Wenliang who had died before were in the same department. Deputy Director and Chief Physician of Ophthalmology Hospital. <br>

【China】 <br>
* The National Health and Construction Commission issued [Notice on Printing and Distributing New Coronavirus Pneumonia Diagnosis and Treatment Program (Trial Version 7)](http://www.gov.cn/zhengce/zhengceku/2020-03/04/content_5486705.htm), indicating Relevant medical institutions should actively play the role of traditional Chinese medicine in medical treatment, strengthen the integration of traditional Chinese and western medicine, improve the system of joint consultation of traditional Chinese and western medicine, and promote medical treatment to achieve good results. <br>
* Zhejiang Province announced the epidemic situation of new coronavirus pneumonia and added 7 imported confirmed cases from abroad (Italy). The 7 cases were close contacts with the first overseas imported case, Wang Moumou, working in the same restaurant in Bergamo, Italy. Eight people have been living in Italy and have no history of contact with Wuhan, Hubei. <br>
* Beijing New Crown Epidemic Prevention and Control Work Press Conference: Beijing Municipal Deputy Secretary-General Chen Bei said that there have been more than 20 Chinese students studying in Iran who have returned home from the Beijing port recently. Those who entered the country through South Korea, Italy, Iran, Japan and other countries with serious epidemic situations, if they are transferred to other places, do the epidemic prevention in strict accordance with local regulations; if the destination is Beijing, whether it is Chinese or foreign , We must implement isolation observation. <br>
* In response to the online report, "The leadership of Ankang City Central Hospital is more amazing than the aid of the first line of Hubei Province", [Shaanxi Ankang City Central Hospital](http://61.134.48.218:8077/content_21_999.html) apologized and said The scope, days and standards of the subsidies for the front-line staff of the hospital were carefully reviewed and strictly checked. On March 2, a statistical table of temporary work subsidies issued by Ankang Central Hospital for frontline epidemic prevention and control personnel was spread online. The table shows that the subsidy standard is 200 yuan and 300 yuan per person per day, the maximum subsidy time is 42 days, and the subsidy amount is 12,600 yuan. Some insiders pointed out that the list includes many hospital leaders, and their subsidies are higher than those of the frontline personnel including the support of Hubei medical care. The list caused controversy. <br>

【International】 <br>
* Beginning on February 22, Moscow law enforcement officers conduct "sudden inspections" in subway stations, buses, and even private houses every day. As of today, Moscow has confirmed that 88 people have violated the segregation system, of which 80 are Chinese citizens. Most of these 80 Chinese people were isolated at the Tsaritsino Rehabilitation Center for the Disabled in southeastern Moscow. As of 10 pm on February 29, Tsaritsino still had about 70 Chinese people stranded. [North Qingshen once](https://www.sohu.com/a/377331858_148781) The reporter interviewed several parties and they restored their experience in Moscow. Some people said that they were “unconsciously” without their knowledge. In violation of the quarantine law, some people are suspected of breaking the law by going out and dumping garbage, and some are suspected of breaking the law by going to the supermarket to buy things. Now they may face the punishment of being deported and not allowed to enter Russia for 5 years. <br>

## March 4, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
* Ms. Mei from Qiaokou District, Wuhan told [Peng Pao News](https://archive.li/wip/TK7rP) that her husband Li Liang, 36 years old this year, was diagnosed as a new coronary pneumonia patient, treated, 2 He was discharged from the sheltered hospital on 26th, and was isolated at the designated rehabilitation point of the hotel. On March 2, he suddenly became ill at the rehabilitation point and died after being sent to hospital. An expert from the Chinese Center for Disease Control believed that Li Liang was discharged from the hospital too early. "There are still images of typical new coronary pneumonia on CT on the 23rd." See March 5 [Caixin.com:Fuyang Suyun: The beginning and end of death after discharge of Xinguan patients](https://github.com/Pratitya/wuhan2020-timeline/issues/145) <br>
* In the evening, a person in charge of Wuhan Jiangan Fangcai Hospital confirmed to [Peng Pai News](https://m.thepaper.cn/newsDetail_forward_6321807) that Jiangan Fangcai Hospital issued an "Emergency Notice": Recently Discharged Patients There were many relapses, which led to re-admission to hospital. The hospital decided that all patients who were to be discharged from the cabin will be tested for virus antibodies Ig-M and Ig-G on the same day. The above inspection will start tomorrow (March 5). <br>

【China】 <br>
* [Hong Kong Fisheries and Conservation Department](https://www.info.gov.hk/gia/general/202003/04/P2020030400656.htm): A dog showed a weak positive response to repeated tests against new coronavirus, The results show that the dog has been infected with the new corona virus to a low degree. The Department has consulted experts from the School of Public Health of the University of Hong Kong, the School of Animal Medicine and Life Sciences of the City University of Hong Kong, and the World Organization for Animal Health. They all agreed that it may be transmitted by humans. The dog does not currently have any symptoms related to new pneumonia and is currently undergoing quarantine at the animal residence of the Hong Kong-Zhuhai-Macao Bridge Port. <br>
* [Peng Pao News](https://weibo.com/5044281310/Ix3cjDAIT) learned from the Central Political and Law Commission that the investigation team conducted a comprehensive investigation on the outbreak of Rencheng Prison in Shandong Province. The outbreak of Rencheng Prison was initiated in January. On the 21st, people who arrived in Jining, Shandong by self-driving car from Wuhan were transmitted to prison officers and employees, which in turn caused infection to some police officers and criminals. <br>
* [Peng Pao News](https://weibo.com/1642088277/Ix57d2Cs5): Beijing Ditan Hospital announced that the first patient with new coronary pneumonia and encephalitis was discharged from the hospital on February 25th. Liu Jingyuan, director of the ICU of the hospital, reminded that patients with consciousness disorders must consider the possibility of viruses attacking the central nervous system. At present, patients with new coronary pneumonia may be complicated by multiple organ damage such as severe respiratory distress syndrome (ARDS), myocardial damage, abnormal coagulation function, kidney damage, liver damage, but no reports of central nervous system involvement have been found. This case report This is the first case in the world. <br>
* [Xinhua Viewpoint](https://m.weibo.cn/1699432410/4478851872453492): Heilongjiang Province held a meeting of the Provincial Committee Standing Committee to decide on the level of emergency response to the prevention and control of the new coronary pneumonia epidemic in Heilongjiang Province. Level 1 emergency response is adjusted to level 2 emergency response. <br>

The deceased was a 75-year-old man who had traveled to the city of Cremona in Lombardy, where the epidemic was severe, to meet relatives and friends. After verification, when implementing the temporary work subsidy policy for the new-level coronary pneumonia frontline epidemic prevention and control staff, the central hospital simply calculated the leadership of the hospital in the expert group as full attendance, and other staff as the attendance calculation, resulting in The issue of "the hospital leadership's anti-epidemic subsidies is higher than the aid to the frontline personnel in Hubei". Chen Wenqian and Dong Genwen were dismissed, and Wang Longjun, the director of the Municipal Health Commission, was exhorted. <br>
* In the afternoon, Wang Guangfa, a member of the expert group of the National Health and Health Commission, pointed out to the [Beijing News](http://www.bjnews.com.cn/feature/2020/03/05/699575.html) that the patient "false negative ", There is the possibility of" Fuyang "after discharge from the hospital, but this is mainly due to sampling errors, and the probability is small. If there is no obvious symptoms of new coronary pneumonia, it is not appropriate to conclude the "new coronary pneumonia recurrence" prematurely. <br>

## March 8, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
* [Cover News](https://weibo.com/1496814565/IxDCRcpSo): Recently, an official seal of the receipt of segregation fees caused controversy on the Internet: 2 Wuhan Huoshenshan Hospital Assistance Workers, Xishui County, Hubei After returning to his hometown, he was arranged for centralized isolation at a local hotel. The town government collected a centralized isolation fee of 4,200 yuan through a labor service company at a standard of 150 yuan / day. On March 8th, Hubei Xishui County official responded that after investigation, the collection of segregation fees of the labor service company by the government of Xima Town was true and the behavior was wrong. We feel deeply guilty and guilty. The fee payment was refunded to the labor service company on the morning of March 7, and an apology was given to the person concerned. <br>

* [Qingshan Government Affairs](https://weibo.com/2758671832/IyafB0nrL): At 17:00 on March 11, the Internet reflects the use of environmental sanitation vehicles by the Qingshan District Steel City Administrative Committee to deliver concentrated purchases of affordable meat for residents. After preliminary understanding, the Steel Metropolitan Administrative Committee used sanitation vehicles to deliver 1,000 copies of cheap meat, and 530 copies have been distributed to residents. After discovering the incident, the Gangdu Management Committee issued an apology letter to the residents, set up six working groups to apologize, recovered the parity meat that had been issued, and promised to deliver the same amount of parity meat to the residents' homes safely and cleanly tomorrow morning. Based on this, the Qingshan Discipline Inspection Commission and the district committee approved the decision, and decided to dismiss Xu Zengtang, secretary of the Party Committee of Gangdu Management Committee, and Zhou Lei, the party committee member and deputy director of the management committee, and filed a case review. Luo Rong's party discipline case review. <br>

That night caused strong dissatisfaction among the masses, surrounded police cars and demanded the release of volunteers. Afterwards [Xiaogan release](https://weibo.com/1642512402/Iyn4XAzDT?ref=collection) notified the "Notes on the gathering of people in the Haishan community of Yingcheng": around 19:30 on March 12 100 people gathered at the basketball court in the community. After being dissuaded by the scene, they dispersed themselves around 20:00. After investigation, there were 3689 households and 8012 people in Haishan District. During the epidemic prevention and control period, Haishan District implemented fully closed management, and simultaneously implemented a unified purchasing and distribution service for residents' daily life supplies, which was implemented by community-organized properties. It was strictly forbidden for others to sell life supplies privately. On March 12, the owner Cheng Mou contacted the merchants to sell vegetables in the community in the name of Caring Vegetables. When the community property stopped and called the police, the prevention and control patrol team rushed to the scene for disposal, which caused the residents of the community to watch. After the incident, the relevant city leaders quickly rushed to the scene for disposal, the personnel dispersed immediately, and the community returned to normal. <br>

Wang Yaoping, deputy director of the Yueyang City Health and Health Committee, said that there have been recent rumors that the Miluo City and the Quyuan Management District caused a cluster infection due to dinner. During the screening of relevant departments, 5 asymptomatic infected persons were found in close contacts. At present, the above five people have no fever, cough and respiratory symptoms. Pulmonary imaging examination revealed no signs of viral pneumonia infection. Nearly 100 close contacts are in good health. As of March 13, Yueyang had no new confirmed cases for 24 consecutive days. <br>
* [Hangzhou Daily](http://www.hangzhou.gov.cn/art/2020/3/13/art_812262_42266038.html): Hangzhou, Zhejiang, reported on March 13 that an asymptomatic infected person had been exposed to a high-risk country. <br>
* [Ping An Beijing](https://weibo.com/1288915263/IySTenHjd): Beijing reported one confirmed case imported from the United States, Limou, female, 37 years old, permanently settled in Massachusetts, USA. On March 14th and 15th, the Municipal Center for Disease Control and Air China announced at the press conference on the prevention and control of the New Coronary Pneumonia Outbreak in Beijing that Li had developed fever, cough and other symptoms during his stay in the United States, and he had been to the local doctor many times. In the United States, he took antipyretics before boarding the plane. After boarding, he did not truthfully provide flight attendants with personal health conditions and the situation of his husband, son and other peers, which caused the risk of infection for the same plane. After receiving the relevant clues, the Beijing police quickly launched an investigation and obtained evidence. After preliminary work, the Shunyi Public Security Branch Bureau has filed an investigation against Li for suspected of obstructing the prevention and treatment of infectious diseases. Currently, Li Mou is undergoing treatment at a designated hospital, and her husband and son are under quarantine observation. <br>
* [South China Morning Post](https://www.zaobao.com.sg/realtime/china/story20200313-1036762): Chinese government non-public documents show that China ’s first patient with 2019 coronavirus disease can be traced back to November 17, last year However, the official known that 266 cases were diagnosed last year, all received medical observation, and some cases are most likely to be backfilled after the sample was collected at the relevant health institution. According to documents obtained by the newspaper, a 55-year-old man from Hubei Province may be the first patient to be infected with coronary disease. The date of diagnosis was as early as November 17. From that day on, the relevant authorities reported one to five confirmed cases every day. As of December 15, the total number had reached 27. The number of diagnoses on a single day also appeared in double digits on December 17, and as of the 20th of the month, the total reached 60 cases. ## March 19, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
* At about 19 o'clock, Xinhua News Agency issued the National Supervision Committee Investigation Team ["Notice on Surveys Relating to Investigations Related to Dr. Li Wenliang"](http://www.ccdi.gov.cn/toutiao/202003/t20200319_213880.html) , Explained the basic situation of Dr. Li Wenliang and the background of forwarding, publishing information about WeChat, receiving public security organs' talks, admonishing and hospital talks, morbidity, treatment, and rescue. It also shows that due to the improper admonishment issued by Zhongnan Road Police Station and irregular law enforcement procedures, the investigation team has recommended that the Wuhan Municipal Supervision Authority in Hubei Province supervise and rectify the matter, urge the public security organ to revoke the admonishment and hold relevant personnel accountable, and promptly announce it to the public process result. <br>
* At the same time, the Xinhua News Agency issued ["The National Supervisory Commission Head of Investigation Team Answers Questions"](https://baijiahao.baidu.com/s?id=1661593507575013144), saying "It is worth noting that some of the hostile forces are in order to attack The Communist Party of China and the Chinese government have labeled Dr. Li Wenliang as a "hero awakener" against the system. This is completely untrue. Li Wenliang is a Communist Party member, not a so-called "anti-system person". Those with ulterior motives The forces want to fan the flames, confuse people, and provoke social emotions, doomed not to succeed. "<br>

The results of the first 7 tests were negative, but a partial positive reaction occurred during the 8th test. Since the high school student died on the morning of the 18th, the Korean Department of Disease Management will conduct a final examination on him. If he is diagnosed as being infected with the new coronavirus, he will be the first minor in Korea to die happily after being infected with the new coronavirus, and it will also be the first death case of the new coronavirus without underlying disease in South Korea. <br>

After a comprehensive investigation, Zhang Moumou, a resident of Kangcheng District, Lishui, Hanjiadun Street Comprehensive Community, is 62 years old. On March 17, he went to the hospital due to a lymph node mass (large neck disease), with normal body temperature and no fever and cough. The first nucleic acid test of the new crown was negative. The second nucleic acid test was positive on March 19 and was admitted to the hospital. According to the "Notice of the General Office of the National Health and Health Commission on Printing and Distributing the New Coronavirus Pneumonia Prevention and Control Program (Sixth Edition)", Zhang Moumou is an asymptomatic infected person, not a confirmed case. The patient's sputum and pharyngeal swabs were collected again on March 20, and the nucleic acid tests were negative. On the evening of March 19, the community learned that Zhang Moumou's second nucleic acid test was positive and mistakenly thought it was a diagnosed patient. In order to remind the community residents to do home prevention and control and raise vigilance, a notice was issued in the community. On the afternoon of March 20, the community explained to the residents of the community that it was not a confirmed patient. <br>

At noon on March 17, some residents of the Qiaobei community, out of vigilance about the community and their own safety, contacted the community grid members and volunteers to ask about their status and health. During this period, a resident expressed that he did not understand that the nurse was not a resident of the jurisdiction or a tenant in the community but moved into the community and dialed 110 to call the police. After the police station issued the police, it handled it properly and persuaded the residents to return. The nurse lived separately in the company of colleagues. Afterwards, our district quickly pointed out the inappropriate behavior of the community, and arranged the streets and the community to take the initiative to communicate with the nurse to explain and obtain their own understanding. <br>

## March 29, 2020
【Wuhan-Hubei】 <br>
【China】 <br>
* [CCTV News](https://weibo.com/2656274875/IAPbXDebJ): Academician Zhong Nanshan accepted an interview with China International Television reporter Tian Wei and said: At present, the situation of "asymptomatic infected people" in China is very limited: both There are no specific figures and no detailed studies. However, based on known facts, some inferences can also be made. For example, generally speaking, the asymptomatic infections have a high infection rate for people who are in close contact with them, but the number of newly diagnosed cases of new coronary pneumonia in China has not only not increased, but has been steadily decreasing, which can explain: China has not yet a large number of " Asymptomatic infection". <br>
* [Second Branch of Beijing Municipal People's Procuratorate](https://weibo.com/1618051664/IAH4hoihL) approves the arrest of the criminal suspect Guo Moumou on suspicion of intentional injury. The suspect Guo Moumou was released from prison. At 15 o'clock on March 14, 2020, Guo Moumou took off his mask while checking out in a supermarket in Dongcheng District, Beijing. The customer Duan Moumou (male, aged 72) reminded him to follow the epidemic prevention regulations and wear a mask, which caused Dissatisfied with Guo Moumou, he dropped Duan Moumou to the ground and hit Duan's head and neck with both hands, causing Duan Moumou to be injured. During the escape from the scene, Guo Moumou wounded two supermarket employees and was arrested on the spot. The victim Duan Moumou died of March 20, 2020 due to a craniocerebral injury, which was invalid after treatment. <br>
* [Henan Health and Health Commission](https://weibo.com/5594618028/IAQ9dcXi8): From 0:00 to 24:00 on March 28, 1 new case of local diagnosis of new coronary pneumonia was added in Henan Province, and the patient was Wang Moumou, Luohe City . Epidemiological investigation found that Wang Moumou took a long-distance bus at Luohe Bus Station at about 10:00 on March 21 to Jiaxian East Bus Station in Pingdingshan City and drove with his Jiaxian classmate Zhang Moumou (Jianxian People's Hospital Doctor) Accompanied to sweep the graves in the countryside, and dine with Zhang Moumou 3 times during Jia County. Continuing the investigation, Zhang Moumou and Liu Moumou, Zhou Moumou (the two are also doctors of Jiaxian People's Hospital) and other people were eating at the same table on the evening of March 13. Liu Moumou had a history of traveling in Wuhan. After returning to Jiao, he quarantined himself for 14 days. <br>
* [Gansu Health and Health Commission](http://wsjk.gansu.gov.cn/single/10910/85032.html): Gansu added one new case of Hubei imported new pneumonia. The case returned to Lanzhou on March 22 by driving from Xianning City, Hubei Province (low-risk area) with the Hubei Health Code "Green Code". From the 23rd, it was left to focus on medical observation and observation. On the 28th, the CT results showed that the inside of the middle lung The segmental and left lung tongue lobe showed a small piece of ground glass exudation, which was officially confirmed after a positive viral nucleic acid test on the 29th. <br>

Based on the epidemic prevention and control situation, Hubei Province and Beijing City can study and put forward opinions on the timetable for college entrance examinations in the region, and the Ministry of Commerce and Education will release them to the society in a timely manner after consent. <br>
* [People's Daily](https://weibo.com/2803301701/IBaklDK9m): Chang Jile, Director of the CDC of the National Health and Health Commission, said that for asymptomatic patients, the case investigation and close contacts must be completed within 24 hours Registration is reported through the system. Strict isolation management. After 14 days of centralized isolation, two negative nucleic acid tests will release the isolation. If positive, continue isolation and observation. Those who are asymptomatically in close contact should also be quarantined for 14 days. From April 1, the daily outbreak bulletin will announce the situation of asymptomatic infected persons. <br>
* [National Health and Health Commission](http://www.nhc.gov.cn/jkj/s3578/202003/718c79c96f3e46409dd49303d41a00ef.shtml) released the "Questions and Answers on the Prevention and Control of Asymptomatic Infections of New Coronavirus": Up to 3 At 24 o'clock on the 30th, 1541 cases of asymptomatic infections under medical observation in China, including 205 cases imported from abroad. Previously, Zhong Nanshan said that the situation of "asymptomatic infected people" in China is currently very limited, and there are no specific figures [see entry on March 29]. <br>
* In the afternoon, the [Drug Supervision Department of the State Food and Drug Administration](http://www.nmpa.gov.cn/WS04/CL2056/376194.html) held a video conference on the key tasks of post-market drug regulatory work in 2020. The meeting emphasized that the drug regulatory departments at all levels should implement the decision-making and deployment of the Party Central Committee and the State Council, resolutely do a good job in the quality control of drugs related to epidemic prevention and control, and request that the quality control of exported drugs be properly done and strictly regulate the management of drug export certification. In compliance with the conditions and requirements for issuing certificates, and failure to comply with China's pharmaceutical GMP, resolutely revoke their drug export certificates; continue to strengthen drug production supervision and ensure that the quality of exported drugs meets the requirements; and strengthen coordination with market supervision, customs, public security and other departments To severely crack down on violations of laws and regulations. <br>
* [Ministry of Commerce, General Administration of Customs, State Food and Drug Administration](http://www.gov.cn/zhengce/zhengceku/2020-04/01/content_5497878.htm) issued a joint document, exporting from April 1 Enterprises with new coronavirus detection reagents, medical masks, medical protective clothing, ventilators, and infrared thermometers must provide written or electronic declarations when they declare to the customs, promising to export products that have obtained China's medical device product registration certificate, in line with the importing country (region) Quality standards. The customs shall check and release the medical device product registration certificate approved by the drug supervision and administration department. Earlier, it was reported that 30% of Spanish imports of Chinese testing reagents failed. <br>

Guangzhou Baiyun Police immediately dispatched personnel to the scene for disposal. After a preliminary investigation: At 7:20 that day, the female nurse Wang Mou of the isolation ward of the Eighth Hospital of the city asked a foreign patient with a new diagnosis of new coronary pneumonia OKONKWONWOYE CHIKA PATRICK (male, 47 years old, Nigerian) to take a blood test, and the patient ignored it. He immediately followed and tried to walk out of the isolation ward. Upon seeing this, the nurse immediately stopped him and was pushed to the ground and beaten and bit his face. After forensic examination, nurse Wang Mou found injuries on his face, neck and waist, and was identified as a minor injury. The foreign-diagnosed patient entered Guangzhou from abroad on March 20 and was tested positive for new coronavirus nucleic acid, and was sent to the eight hospitals of the city for isolation treatment on the 23rd. At present, its nucleic acid test is still positive. <br>

The notice made it clear that registration will first be open to qualified primary and secondary students in the United States. * The Civil Aviation Administration of China and the General Administration of Customs of the People's Republic of China released today [Announcement on Filling in Health Information for Epidemic Prevention before Chinese Passengers Return to China by Flight](http://www.gov.cn/zhengce/zhengceku/2020-04/07 /content_5500034.htm), the specific requirements are as follows: 1. From April 8, 2020, passengers who have purchased tickets need to pass the WeChat mini program of the international version of the anti-epidemic health code in advance before boarding the plane, and fill in their personal data, health status, recent status daily Information such as travel conditions. Special circumstances can be reported by others. 2. The transition period is from April 8 to April 22, 2020. Chinese passengers taking a flight during the transition period should report on consecutive days starting from April 8. If you take a flight after the transition period, you should fill in the report day by day from the 14th day before boarding. 3. If you fail to fill in the above requirements, you will not be able to board the plane. Passengers filling in false information will cause the itinerary to be blocked and must bear corresponding legal responsibilities. <br>

* [State Council](http://www.gov.cn/zhengce/content/2020-04/08/content_5500371.htm) issued the management regulations for asymptomatic infected persons: strengthened the management of asymptomatic infected persons. It indicates that there is a risk of transmission of asymptomatic infections; those who are found to be asymptomatic should report directly to the Internet within 2 hours; those with asymptomatic infections should be concentrated in medical observation for 14 days; those who have been in concentrated medical observation for 14 days and two consecutive negative nucleic acid tests (The sampling time should be at least 24 hours apart.) Centralized medical observation can be lifted. Those who still have a positive nucleic acid test and no clinical symptoms need to continue concentrated medical observation. <br>

Today, 866 people return to Beijing by high-speed rail. Persons stranded in Wuhan and Beijing need to perform a nucleic acid test within 7 days before returning to Beijing. The result is negative before they can buy high-speed rail tickets or return to Beijing by car. <br>

(2) Body temperature detection equipment: fully automatic infrared body temperature detector, hand-held infrared thermometer. (3) Anti-killing materials: medical alcohol, 84 disinfectant, medical hand sanitizer and other related materials. <br>

* [CCTV News](https://weibo.com/2656274875/IDB77g4wI?type=comment): Bao Liqun, deputy general manager of China Railway Wuhan Bureau Group Co., Ltd .: Recently, we found that some passengers carry alcohol for personal protection , Disinfectant and other prohibited items enter the station. 【China】 <br>
* [Life Times](https://www.weibo.com/1774057271/IDoKAp8H4?refer_flag=1001030103_&type=comment#_rnd1587009582758): China is already in Wuhan, Beijing, Shanghai, Chongqing, Liaoning Province in the northeast, and Jiangsu on the east coast Large-scale epidemiological investigations of new coronaviruses have been initiated in nine provinces and cities in the provinces and Zhejiang Province, southern Guangdong Province and western Sichuan Province. This survey will be the first in the world to cover such a wide area, and aims to assess the scale and immunity of asymptomatic people in the population. The survey will include collecting throat swabs for virus testing and using antibody testing to determine whether antibodies have been produced in residents. Wuhan will select 11,000 out of 11 million residents for investigation, and plans to complete sampling on Thursday. [See entry on April 14] According to the China Daily, the participants in this investigation are mainly ordinary residents and a small number of "epidemic prevention and control staff", such as security guards and taxi drivers. <br>
* [Capital Health](https://weibo.com/2417852083/IDy1f63j8): From 0:00 to 24:00 on April 15th, there are no new reports of imported confirmed cases, suspected cases and asymptomatic infections of new coronary pneumonia imported from abroad, cured and discharged 8 cases. <br>
